           <td class="blob-line-code"><div class="code-body highlight"><pre><div class='line' id='LC1'>*csupport.txt*                  C/C++ Support                January 06 2012</div><div class='line' id='LC2'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC3'>C/C++ Support                                           *c-support* *csupport*</div><div class='line' id='LC4'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Plugin version 5.18</div><div class='line' id='LC5'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for Vim version 7.0 and above</div><div class='line' id='LC6'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Fritz Mehner  &lt;mehner@fh-swf.de&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC7'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC8'>C/C++-IDE for Vim/gVim. It is written to considerably speed up writing code in</div><div class='line' id='LC9'>a consistent style.  This is done by inserting complete statements,idioms,</div><div class='line' id='LC10'>code snippets, templates, and comments.  Syntax checking, compiling,  running</div><div class='line' id='LC11'>a program, running a code checker or a reformatter can be done with a</div><div class='line' id='LC12'>keystroke.</div><div class='line' id='LC13'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC14'>&nbsp;1.    Usage                                    |csupport-usage-gvim|</div><div class='line' id='LC15'>&nbsp;1.1    Menu &#39;Comments&#39;                         |csupport-comm|</div><div class='line' id='LC16'>&nbsp;1.1.1   Append aligned comments                |csupport-comm-aligned|</div><div class='line' id='LC17'>&nbsp;1.1.2   Adjust end-of-line comments            |csupport-comm-realign|</div><div class='line' id='LC18'>&nbsp;1.1.3   Code to comment                        |csupport-code-to-comm|</div><div class='line' id='LC19'>&nbsp;1.1.4   Comment to code                        |csupport-comm-to-code|</div><div class='line' id='LC20'>&nbsp;1.1.5   Frame comments, file header, ...       |csupport-comm-frame|</div><div class='line' id='LC21'>&nbsp;1.1.6   File section comments         ..       |csupport-comm-sections|</div><div class='line' id='LC22'>&nbsp;1.1.7   Keyword comment, special comment       |csupport-comm-keyword|</div><div class='line' id='LC23'>&nbsp;1.1.8   Tags (plugin)                          |csupport-comm-tags|</div><div class='line' id='LC24'>&nbsp;1.1.9   Date and date+time                     |csupport-comm-date|</div><div class='line' id='LC25'>&nbsp;1.1.10  C to C++ comments and vice versa       |csupport-comm-c-cpp|</div><div class='line' id='LC26'>&nbsp;1.2    Menu &#39;Statements&#39;                       |csupport-stat|</div><div class='line' id='LC27'>&nbsp;1.2.1   Normal mode, insert mode.              |csupport-stat-normal-mode|</div><div class='line' id='LC28'>&nbsp;1.2.2   Visual mode.                           |csupport-stat-visual-mode|</div><div class='line' id='LC29'>&nbsp;1.3    Menu &#39;Preprocessor&#39;                     |csupport-prep|</div><div class='line' id='LC30'>&nbsp;1.3.1   Normal mode, insert mode.              |csupport-prep-normal-mode|</div><div class='line' id='LC31'>&nbsp;1.3.2   Visual mode.                           |csupport-prep-visual-mode|</div><div class='line' id='LC32'>&nbsp;1.3.3   Block out code with #if 0 .. #endif    |csupport-prep-if0|</div><div class='line' id='LC33'>&nbsp;1.3.4   Ex-commands                            |csupport-prep-ex|</div><div class='line' id='LC34'>&nbsp;1.4    Menu &#39;Idioms&#39;                           |csupport-idioms|</div><div class='line' id='LC35'>&nbsp;1.4.1   Item &#39;function&#39;                        |csupport-idioms-function|</div><div class='line' id='LC36'>&nbsp;1.4.2   for-loop control                       |csupport-idioms-for-loop|</div><div class='line' id='LC37'>&nbsp;1.4.3   Item &#39;open input file&#39;                 |csupport-idioms-input|</div><div class='line' id='LC38'>&nbsp;1.4.4   Item &#39;open output file&#39;                |csupport-idioms-output|</div><div class='line' id='LC39'>&nbsp;1.5    Menu &#39;Snippets&#39;                         |csupport-snippets|</div><div class='line' id='LC40'>&nbsp;1.5.1   Code snippets                          |csupport-snippets|</div><div class='line' id='LC41'>&nbsp;1.5.2   Picking up prototypes                  |csupport-proto|</div><div class='line' id='LC42'>&nbsp;1.5.3   Code templates                         |csupport-templates-menu|</div><div class='line' id='LC43'>&nbsp;1.6    Menu &#39;C++&#39;                              |csupport-c++|</div><div class='line' id='LC44'>&nbsp;1.6.1   Normal mode, insert mode.              |csupport-c++-normal-mode|</div><div class='line' id='LC45'>&nbsp;1.6.2   Visual mode.                           |csupport-c++-visual-mode|</div><div class='line' id='LC46'>&nbsp;1.6.3   Method implementation                  |csupport-c++-method-impl|</div><div class='line' id='LC47'>&nbsp;1.6.4  Ex commands                             |csupport-c++-ex|</div><div class='line' id='LC48'>&nbsp;1.7    Menu &#39;Run&#39;                              |csupport-run|</div><div class='line' id='LC49'>&nbsp;1.7.1   Minimal make functionality             |csupport-run-buffer|</div><div class='line' id='LC50'>&nbsp;1.7.2   Command line arguments                 |csupport-run-cmdline-args|</div><div class='line' id='LC51'>&nbsp;1.7.3   Run make                               |csupport-run-make|</div><div class='line' id='LC52'>&nbsp;1.7.4   Choose Makefile                        |csupport-choose-makefile|</div><div class='line' id='LC53'>&nbsp;1.7.4   Executable to run                      |csupport-run-make-run|</div><div class='line' id='LC54'>&nbsp;1.7.6   Run make clean                         |csupport-run-make-clean|</div><div class='line' id='LC55'>&nbsp;1.7.7   Command line arguments for make        |csupport-run-make-args|</div><div class='line' id='LC56'>&nbsp;1.7.8   Splint                                 |csupport-run-splint|</div><div class='line' id='LC57'>&nbsp;1.7.9   CodeCheck                              |csupport-run-codecheck|</div><div class='line' id='LC58'>&nbsp;1.7.10  Indent                                 |csupport-run-indent|</div><div class='line' id='LC59'>&nbsp;1.7.11  Hardcopy                               |csupport-run-hardcopy|</div><div class='line' id='LC60'>&nbsp;1.7.12  Rebuild templates                      |csupport-run-templates|</div><div class='line' id='LC61'>&nbsp;1.7.13  Xterm size                             |csupport-run-xterm|</div><div class='line' id='LC62'>&nbsp;1.7.14  Output redirection                     |csupport-run-output|</div><div class='line' id='LC63'>&nbsp;1.8    Help                                    |csupport-help|</div><div class='line' id='LC64'>&nbsp;</div><div class='line' id='LC65'>&nbsp;2.    Usage without GUI                        |csupport-usage-vim|</div><div class='line' id='LC66'>&nbsp;3.    Hotkeys                                  |csupport-hotkeys|</div><div class='line' id='LC67'>&nbsp;4.    Customization and configuration          |csupport-custom|</div><div class='line' id='LC68'>&nbsp;4.1    Global variables                        |csupport-custom-glob-vars|</div><div class='line' id='LC69'>&nbsp;4.2     The root menu                          |csupport-custom-root|</div><div class='line' id='LC70'>&nbsp;4.3     System-wide installation               |csupport-system-wide|</div><div class='line' id='LC71'>&nbsp;5.    Template files and tags                  |csupport-templates|</div><div class='line' id='LC72'>&nbsp;5.1    Template files                          |csupport-templates-files|</div><div class='line' id='LC73'>&nbsp;5.2    Macros                                  |csupport-templates-macros|</div><div class='line' id='LC74'>&nbsp;5.2.1  User defined formats for date and time  |csupport-templates-date|</div><div class='line' id='LC75'>&nbsp;5.3    Templates                               |csupport-templates-names|</div><div class='line' id='LC76'>&nbsp;5.3.1  Template names                          |csupport-templates-names|</div><div class='line' id='LC77'>&nbsp;5.3.2  Template definition                     |csupport-templates-definition|</div><div class='line' id='LC78'>&nbsp;5.3.3  Template expansion                      |csupport-templates-expansion|</div><div class='line' id='LC79'>&nbsp;5.3.4  The macros &lt;+text+&gt; etc.                |csupport-templates-jump|</div><div class='line' id='LC80'>&nbsp;5.3.5  Command Ctrl-j                          |csupport-Ctrl-j|</div><div class='line' id='LC81'>&nbsp;5.4    Switching between template sets         |csupport-templates-sets|</div><div class='line' id='LC82'>&nbsp;5.5    Binding a style to a file extension     |csupport-templates-bind|</div><div class='line' id='LC83'>&nbsp;6.    C/C++ Dictionaries                       |csupport-dictionary|</div><div class='line' id='LC84'>&nbsp;7.    Extend ctags                             |csupport-ctags|</div><div class='line' id='LC85'>&nbsp;7.1   Make and qmake                           |csupport-ctags-make|</div><div class='line' id='LC86'>&nbsp;7.2   Templates                                |csupport-ctags-templates|</div><div class='line' id='LC87'>&nbsp;8.    Folding                                  |csupport-folding|</div><div class='line' id='LC88'>&nbsp;9     Additional Mappings                      |csupport-ad-mappings|</div><div class='line' id='LC89'>&nbsp;10.   Windows particularities                  |csupport-windows|</div><div class='line' id='LC90'>&nbsp;11.   Additional tips                          |csupport-tips|</div><div class='line' id='LC91'>&nbsp;12.   Troubleshooting                          |csupport-troubleshooting|</div><div class='line' id='LC92'>&nbsp;13.   Release Notes /Change Log                |csupport-release-notes|</div><div class='line' id='LC93'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC94'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;How to add this help file to Vim&#39;s help  |add-local-help|</div><div class='line' id='LC95'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC96'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC97'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC98'>1.  USAGE WITH GUI  (gVim)                               *csupport-usage-gvim*</div><div class='line' id='LC99'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC100'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC101'>If the root menu &#39;C/C++&#39; is not visible call it with the item &quot;Load C Support&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC102'>from the standard Tools-menu.</div><div class='line' id='LC103'>The item &quot;Load C Support&quot; can also be used to unload the C/C++-root menu.</div><div class='line' id='LC104'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC105'>Nearly all menu entries insert code snippets or comments. All of these are</div><div class='line' id='LC106'>contained within template files and can be changed by the user to meet their</div><div class='line' id='LC107'>requirements (see|csupport-templates|).</div><div class='line' id='LC108'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC109'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC110'>1.1  MENU &#39;Comments&#39;                                           *csupport-comm*</div><div class='line' id='LC111'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC112'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC113'>1.1.1  APPEND ALIGNED COMMENTS TO CONSECUTIVE LINES    *csupport-comm-aligned*</div><div class='line' id='LC114'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC115'>In NORMAL MODE, the menu item &#39;end-of-line comment&#39; will append a comment to</div><div class='line' id='LC116'>the current line.</div><div class='line' id='LC117'>In VISUAL MODE, this item will append aligned comments to all marked lines.</div><div class='line' id='LC118'>Marking the first 4 lines</div><div class='line' id='LC119'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC120'>&nbsp;&nbsp;print_double_array ( double array[],</div><div class='line' id='LC121'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;int    n,</div><div class='line' id='LC122'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;int    columns,</div><div class='line' id='LC123'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;char*  arrayname</div><div class='line' id='LC124'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;)</div><div class='line' id='LC125'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC126'>and choosing &#39;end-of-line com. /**/&#39; will yield.</div><div class='line' id='LC127'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC128'>&nbsp;&nbsp;print_double_array ( double array[],          /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC129'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;int    n,                /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC130'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;int    columns,          /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC131'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;char*  arrayname         /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC132'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;)                        /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC133'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC134'>If one or more lines go beyond the starting column (s.below), the comments</div><div class='line' id='LC135'>will start at the second column after the longest line.  The cursor will then</div><div class='line' id='LC136'>be positioned inside the first comment.</div><div class='line' id='LC137'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC138'>The default starting column is 49 ( = (multiple of 2,4, or 8) + 1 ).  This can</div><div class='line' id='LC139'>be changed by setting a global variable in the file ~/.vimrc , e.g. :</div><div class='line' id='LC140'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC141'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_LineEndCommColDefault    = 45</div><div class='line' id='LC142'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC143'>The starting column can also be set by the menu item</div><div class='line' id='LC144'>&#39;Comments-&gt;set end-of-line com. col&#39;.  Just position the cursor in an</div><div class='line' id='LC145'>arbitrary column (column number is shown in the Vim status line) and choose</div><div class='line' id='LC146'>this menu item.  This setting is buffer related.</div><div class='line' id='LC147'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC148'>If the cursor was at the end of a line you will be asked for a column number</div><div class='line' id='LC149'>because this position is most likely not the desired starting column.</div><div class='line' id='LC150'>Your choice will be confirmed.</div><div class='line' id='LC151'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC152'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC153'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC154'>1.1.2  ADJUST END-OF-LINE COMMENTS                    *csupport-comm-realign*</div><div class='line' id='LC155'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC156'>After some changes end-of-line comments may be no longer aligned:</div><div class='line' id='LC157'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC158'>&nbsp;&nbsp;print_double_array ( double       array[],          /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC159'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;long int     n,                     /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC160'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;unsigned int columns,          /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC161'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;char*        a_name         /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC162'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;)                        /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC163'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC164'>Realignment can be achieved with the menu item &#39;adjust end-of-line com.&#39; In</div><div class='line' id='LC165'>normal mode the comment (if any) in the current line will be aligned to the</div><div class='line' id='LC166'>end-of-line comment column (see above) if possible. In visual mode the</div><div class='line' id='LC167'>comments in the marked block will be aligned:</div><div class='line' id='LC168'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC169'>&nbsp;&nbsp;print_double_array ( double       array[],    /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC170'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;long int     n,          /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC171'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;unsigned int columns,    /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC172'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;char*        a_name      /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC173'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;)                        /*  */</div><div class='line' id='LC174'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC175'>The realignment will not be done for comments with nothing else than leading</div><div class='line' id='LC176'>whitespaces. These comments are usually captions:</div><div class='line' id='LC177'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC178'>&nbsp;&nbsp;max = other.max;                    /* the maximum value */</div><div class='line' id='LC179'>&nbsp;&nbsp;len = other.len;                         /* the length        */</div><div class='line' id='LC180'>&nbsp;&nbsp;/* ===== the next section ===== */</div><div class='line' id='LC181'>&nbsp;&nbsp;pos = (x+y+z)/3.0;             /* the next position */</div><div class='line' id='LC182'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC183'>After the alignment we have:</div><div class='line' id='LC184'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC185'>&nbsp;&nbsp;max = other.max;                              /* the maximum value */</div><div class='line' id='LC186'>&nbsp;&nbsp;len = other.len;                              /* the length        */</div><div class='line' id='LC187'>&nbsp;&nbsp;/* ===== the next section ===== */</div><div class='line' id='LC188'>&nbsp;&nbsp;pos = (x+y+z)/3.0;                            /* the next position */</div><div class='line' id='LC189'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC190'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC191'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC192'>1.1.3  CODE TO COMMENT                                 *csupport-code-to-comm*</div><div class='line' id='LC193'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC194'>The marked block</div><div class='line' id='LC195'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC196'>xxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC197'>xxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC198'>xxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC199'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC200'>will be changed by the menu item &#39;code-&gt;comment /**/&#39; into the multiline</div><div class='line' id='LC201'>comment (all (partially) marked lines):</div><div class='line' id='LC202'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC203'>/* xxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC204'>&nbsp;* xxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC205'>&nbsp;* xxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC206'>&nbsp;*/</div><div class='line' id='LC207'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC208'>The marked block will be changed  by the menu item &#39;code-&gt;comment //&#39; into the</div><div class='line' id='LC209'>multiline comment</div><div class='line' id='LC210'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC211'>//xxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC212'>//xxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC213'>//xxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC214'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC215'>The menu items works also for a single line. A single line needs not to be</div><div class='line' id='LC216'>marked.</div><div class='line' id='LC217'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC218'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC219'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC220'>1.1.4  COMMENT TO CODE                                 *csupport-comm-to-code*</div><div class='line' id='LC221'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC222'>If one (or more) complete comment (i.e. all lines belonging to the comment) is</div><div class='line' id='LC223'>marked the item &#39;comment-&gt;code&#39; will uncomment it.  If the following lines</div><div class='line' id='LC224'>are marked</div><div class='line' id='LC225'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC226'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* printf (&quot;\n&quot;);</div><div class='line' id='LC227'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*/</div><div class='line' id='LC228'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC229'>&nbsp;&nbsp;printf (&quot;\n&quot;);</div><div class='line' id='LC230'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC231'>&nbsp;&nbsp;//  printf (&quot;\n&quot;);</div><div class='line' id='LC232'>&nbsp;&nbsp;//</div><div class='line' id='LC233'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC234'>&nbsp;&nbsp;/*</div><div class='line' id='LC235'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*  printf (&quot;\n&quot;);</div><div class='line' id='LC236'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*/</div><div class='line' id='LC237'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC238'>uncommenting will yield</div><div class='line' id='LC239'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC240'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* printf (&quot;\n&quot;);</div><div class='line' id='LC241'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*/</div><div class='line' id='LC242'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC243'>&nbsp;&nbsp;printf (&quot;\n&quot;);</div><div class='line' id='LC244'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC245'>&nbsp;&nbsp;printf (&quot;\n&quot;);</div><div class='line' id='LC246'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC247'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC248'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC249'>&nbsp;&nbsp;printf (&quot;\n&quot;);</div><div class='line' id='LC250'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC251'>The first 2 lines are only a part of a C-comment and remain unchanged.</div><div class='line' id='LC252'>A C-comment can start with /* , /** or /*! .</div><div class='line' id='LC253'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC254'>The menu item works also for a single line with a leading // . A single line</div><div class='line' id='LC255'>needs not to be marked.</div><div class='line' id='LC256'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC257'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC258'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC259'>1.1.5  FRAME COMMENTS, FILE HEADER, ...                  *csupport-comm-frame*</div><div class='line' id='LC260'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC261'>Frame comments, file header comments and function, methods, class descriptions</div><div class='line' id='LC262'>are read as templates from the appropriate files (see |csupport-templates|).</div><div class='line' id='LC263'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC264'>There are two file description templates (menu items &#39;file description (impl.)&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC265'>and  &#39;file description (header)&#39;, see also |csupport-templates|):</div><div class='line' id='LC266'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC267'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-description         : files *.c *.cc *.cp *.cxx *.cpp *.CPP *.c++</div><div class='line' id='LC268'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*.C *.i *.ii </div><div class='line' id='LC269'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC270'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-description-header  : everything else with filetype &#39;c&#39; or &#39;cpp&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC271'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC272'>The appropriate template will also be included into a new file. The plugin </div><div class='line' id='LC273'>decides on the basis of the file extension. The default is shown above. You</div><div class='line' id='LC274'>can change the list by setting a global variable in &#39;~/.vimrc&#39;:</div><div class='line' id='LC275'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC276'>&nbsp;&nbsp;au BufRead,BufNewFile  *.XYZ  set filetype=c</div><div class='line' id='LC277'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC278'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_SourceCodeExtensions  = &#39;XYZ c cc cp cxx cpp CPP c++ C i ii&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC279'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC280'>A new file named &#39;test.XYZ&#39; will now be considered a C implementation file. </div><div class='line' id='LC281'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC282'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC283'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC284'>1.1.6  FILE SECTION COMMENTS                          *csupport-comm-sections*</div><div class='line' id='LC285'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC286'>File section comments can be uses to separate typical C- and H-file sections</div><div class='line' id='LC287'>with comments of similar appearance, e.g.</div><div class='line' id='LC288'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC289'>/* #####   HEADER FILE INCLUDES   ################################################### */</div><div class='line' id='LC290'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC291'>/* #####   MACROS  -  LOCAL TO THIS SOURCE FILE   ################################### */</div><div class='line' id='LC292'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC293'>/* #####   TYPE DEFINITIONS  -  LOCAL TO THIS SOURCE FILE   ######################### */</div><div class='line' id='LC294'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC295'>These section comments can also be inserted using the hotkey \ccs for C/C++</div><div class='line' id='LC296'>files, or \chs for H-files. These hotkeys will start the command</div><div class='line' id='LC297'>&#39;CFileSection&#39; or &#39;HFileSection&#39;  on the command line:</div><div class='line' id='LC298'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC299'>&nbsp;:CFileSection </div><div class='line' id='LC300'>&nbsp;:HFileSection </div><div class='line' id='LC301'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC302'>Now type a &lt;Tab&gt; to start the selection menu to choose from.</div><div class='line' id='LC303'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC304'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC305'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC306'>1.1.7  KEYWORD COMMENT, SPECIAL COMMENT                *csupport-comm-keyword*</div><div class='line' id='LC307'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC308'>Keword comments are end-of-line comments:</div><div class='line' id='LC309'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC310'>&nbsp;/* :&lt;keyword&gt;:&lt;date+time&gt;:&lt;author reference&gt;: &lt;arbitrary comment text&gt; */</div><div class='line' id='LC311'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC312'>Keywords are </div><div class='line' id='LC313'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC314'>&nbsp;BUG COMPILER TODO TRICKY WARNING WORKAROUND user-defined-keyword</div><div class='line' id='LC315'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC316'>These are preliminary comments to document places where work will be resumed</div><div class='line' id='LC317'>shortly. They are usually not meant for the final documentation.  These</div><div class='line' id='LC318'>comments are easily found by searching for the keyword.</div><div class='line' id='LC319'>The keyword comments can also be inserted using the hotkey \ckc . This hotkey</div><div class='line' id='LC320'>starts the command &#39;KeywordComment&#39; on the command line:</div><div class='line' id='LC321'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC322'>&nbsp;:KeywordComment</div><div class='line' id='LC323'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC324'>Now type a &lt;Tab&gt; to start the selection menu to choose from.</div><div class='line' id='LC325'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC326'>Special comments are occasionally used to mark special features of a code</div><div class='line' id='LC327'>construct (e.g. a fall through cases in a switch statement, an empty loop):</div><div class='line' id='LC328'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC329'>&nbsp;/* EMPTY */</div><div class='line' id='LC330'>&nbsp;/* NOT REACHED */</div><div class='line' id='LC331'>&nbsp;/* REMAINS TO BE IMPLEMENTED */</div><div class='line' id='LC332'>&nbsp;&nbsp;....</div><div class='line' id='LC333'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC334'>The special comments can also be inserted using the hotkey \csc . This hotkey</div><div class='line' id='LC335'>starts the command &#39;SpecialComment&#39; on the command line:</div><div class='line' id='LC336'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC337'>&nbsp;:SpecialComment</div><div class='line' id='LC338'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC339'>Now type a &lt;Tab&gt; to start the selection menu to choose from.</div><div class='line' id='LC340'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC341'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC342'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC343'>1.1.8  TAGS (PLUGIN)                                      *csupport-comm-tags*</div><div class='line' id='LC344'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC345'>The submenu &#39;tags (plugin)&#39; let you insert the predefined macros from the</div><div class='line' id='LC346'>template system (see|csupport-templates-macros|). In visual mode the marked</div><div class='line' id='LC347'>string will be replaced by the macro.</div><div class='line' id='LC348'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC349'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC350'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC351'>1.1.9  DATE AND DATE+TIME                                 *csupport-comm-date*</div><div class='line' id='LC352'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC353'>The format for &#39;date&#39; and &#39;date time&#39; can be defined by the user (see</div><div class='line' id='LC354'>|csupport-templates-date|). In visual mode the marked string will be replaced</div><div class='line' id='LC355'>by the macro (e.g. to update date and time).</div><div class='line' id='LC356'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC357'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC358'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC359'>1.1.10 C TO C++ COMMENTS AND VICE VERSA                  *csupport-comm-c-cpp*</div><div class='line' id='LC360'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC361'>The menu item &#39;/* xxx */ &lt;-&gt; // xxx&#39; changes a C++ comment into a C comment</div><div class='line' id='LC362'>and a C++ comment into a C comment (toggle).</div><div class='line' id='LC363'>This is done for the current line in normal or insert mode and for a marked</div><div class='line' id='LC364'>area of lines in visual mode.</div><div class='line' id='LC365'>The hotkey \cx does the same. It can be used with a range:</div><div class='line' id='LC366'>&nbsp;&nbsp;3\cx</div><div class='line' id='LC367'>changes the current line and the next 2 lines.</div><div class='line' id='LC368'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC369'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC370'>1.2  MENU &#39;Statements&#39;                                         *csupport-stat*</div><div class='line' id='LC371'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC372'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC373'>1.2.1  NORMAL MODE, INSERT MODE.                   *csupport-stat-normal-mode*</div><div class='line' id='LC374'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC375'>An empty statement will be inserted and properly indented. The item &#39;if{}&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC376'>will insert an if-statement:</div><div class='line' id='LC377'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC378'>if (  )</div><div class='line' id='LC379'>{</div><div class='line' id='LC380'>}</div><div class='line' id='LC381'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC382'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC383'>1.2.2  VISUAL MODE.                                *csupport-stat-visual-mode*</div><div class='line' id='LC384'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC385'>STATEMENTS WITH BLOCKS AND CASE LABEL.</div><div class='line' id='LC386'>--------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC387'>The highlighted area</div><div class='line' id='LC388'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC389'>xxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC390'>xxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC391'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC392'>can be surrounded by one of the following statements:</div><div class='line' id='LC393'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC394'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+----------------------------+-----------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC395'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|     if (  )                |     if (  )                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC396'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|     {                      |     {                       |</div><div class='line' id='LC397'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|       xxxxx                |       xxxxx                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC398'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|       xxxxx                |       xxxxx                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC399'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|     }                      |     }                       |</div><div class='line' id='LC400'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|                            |     else                    |</div><div class='line' id='LC401'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|                            |     {                       |</div><div class='line' id='LC402'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|                            |     }                       |</div><div class='line' id='LC403'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+----------------------------+-----------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC404'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|     for ( ; ;  )           |     while (  )              |</div><div class='line' id='LC405'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|     {                      |     {                       |</div><div class='line' id='LC406'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|       xxxxx                |       xxxxx                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC407'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|       xxxxx                |       xxxxx                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC408'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|     }                      |     }                       |</div><div class='line' id='LC409'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+----------------------------+-----------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC410'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|     do                     |                             |</div><div class='line' id='LC411'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|     {                      |     {                       |</div><div class='line' id='LC412'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|       xxxxx                |       xxxxx                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC413'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|       xxxxx                |       xxxxx                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC414'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|     }                      |     }                       |</div><div class='line' id='LC415'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|     while (  );            |                             |</div><div class='line' id='LC416'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+----------------------------+-----------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC417'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|      switch (  ) {                                       |</div><div class='line' id='LC418'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|      case :                                              |</div><div class='line' id='LC419'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|       break;                                             |</div><div class='line' id='LC420'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|                                                          |</div><div class='line' id='LC421'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|      case :                                              |</div><div class='line' id='LC422'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|       break;                                             |</div><div class='line' id='LC423'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|                                                          |</div><div class='line' id='LC424'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|      case :                                              |</div><div class='line' id='LC425'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|       break;                                             |</div><div class='line' id='LC426'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|                                                          |</div><div class='line' id='LC427'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|      case :                                              |</div><div class='line' id='LC428'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|       break;                                             |</div><div class='line' id='LC429'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|                                                          |</div><div class='line' id='LC430'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|      default:                                            |</div><div class='line' id='LC431'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|       break;                                             |</div><div class='line' id='LC432'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|      }                                                   |</div><div class='line' id='LC433'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+----------------------------+-----------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC434'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC435'>The whole statement will be indented after insertion.</div><div class='line' id='LC436'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC437'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC438'>STATEMENTS WITHOUT BLOCKS.</div><div class='line' id='LC439'>--------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC440'>One of the following statements can be inserted:</div><div class='line' id='LC441'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC442'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+-------------------------------+--------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC443'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    if (  )                    |    for ( ; ;  )          |</div><div class='line' id='LC444'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+-------------------------------+--------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC445'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    if (  )                    |    while (  )            |</div><div class='line' id='LC446'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    else                       |                          |</div><div class='line' id='LC447'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+-------------------------------+--------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC448'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    case :                     |                          |</div><div class='line' id='LC449'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|      break;                   |                          |</div><div class='line' id='LC450'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+-------------------------------+--------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC451'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC452'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC453'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC454'>1.3  MENU &#39;Preprocessor&#39;                                       *csupport-prep*</div><div class='line' id='LC455'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC456'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC457'>1.3.1  NORMAL MODE, INSERT MODE.                   *csupport-prep-normal-mode*</div><div class='line' id='LC458'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC459'>The preprocessor statements will be inserted and properly indented.</div><div class='line' id='LC460'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC461'>1.3.2  VISUAL MODE.                                *csupport-prep-visual-mode*</div><div class='line' id='LC462'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC463'>STATEMENTS WITH BLOCKS</div><div class='line' id='LC464'>----------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC465'>The highlighted area</div><div class='line' id='LC466'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC467'>xxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC468'>xxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC469'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC470'>can be surrounded by one of the following statements:</div><div class='line' id='LC471'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC472'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+----------------------------+-----------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC473'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #if  CONDITION                                        |</div><div class='line' id='LC474'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    xxxxx                                                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC475'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    xxxxx                                                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC476'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #else      /* ----- #if CONDITION  ----- */           |</div><div class='line' id='LC477'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|                                                          |</div><div class='line' id='LC478'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #endif     /* ----- #if CONDITION  ----- */           |</div><div class='line' id='LC479'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+----------------------------------------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC480'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #ifdef  CONDITION                                     |</div><div class='line' id='LC481'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    xxxxx                                                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC482'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    xxxxx                                                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC483'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #else      /* ----- #ifdef CONDITION  ----- */        |</div><div class='line' id='LC484'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|                                                          |</div><div class='line' id='LC485'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #endif     /* ----- #ifdef CONDITION  ----- */        |</div><div class='line' id='LC486'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+----------------------------------------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC487'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #ifndef  CONDITION                                    |</div><div class='line' id='LC488'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    xxxxx                                                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC489'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    xxxxx                                                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC490'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #else      /* ----- #ifndef CONDITION  ----- */       |</div><div class='line' id='LC491'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|                                                          |</div><div class='line' id='LC492'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #endif     /* ----- #ifndef CONDITION  ----- */       |</div><div class='line' id='LC493'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+----------------------------------------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC494'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #ifndef  INC_TEST                                     |</div><div class='line' id='LC495'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #define  INC_TEST                                     |</div><div class='line' id='LC496'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    xxxxx                                                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC497'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    xxxxx                                                 |</div><div class='line' id='LC498'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #endif   /* ----- #ifndef INC_TEST  ----- */          |</div><div class='line' id='LC499'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+----------------------------------------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC500'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #if  0     /* ----- #if 0 : If0Label_1 ----- */       |</div><div class='line' id='LC501'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|                                                          |</div><div class='line' id='LC502'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|    #endif     /* ----- #if 0 : If0Label_1 ----- */       |</div><div class='line' id='LC503'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+----------------------------------------------------------+</div><div class='line' id='LC504'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC505'>The macro name for an include guard (e.g. INC_TEST above) will be derived as a</div><div class='line' id='LC506'>suggestion from the file name.</div><div class='line' id='LC507'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC508'>1.3.3  BLOCK OUT CODE WITH #if 0 ... #endif                *csupport-prep-if0*</div><div class='line' id='LC509'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC510'>The menu item #if 0 #endif  inserts the lines</div><div class='line' id='LC511'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC512'>&nbsp;&nbsp;#if  0     /* ----- #if 0 : If0Label_1 ----- */</div><div class='line' id='LC513'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC514'>&nbsp;&nbsp;#endif     /* ----- #if 0 : If0Label_1 ----- */</div><div class='line' id='LC515'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC516'>In visual mode the marked block of lines will be surrounded by these lines.</div><div class='line' id='LC517'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC518'>This is usually done to temporarily block out some code.  The label names like</div><div class='line' id='LC519'>If0Label_1 are automatically inserted into the comments.  The trailing numbers</div><div class='line' id='LC520'>are automatically incremented.  These numbers can be changed by the user.  The</div><div class='line' id='LC521'>next number will be one above the highest number found in the current buffer.</div><div class='line' id='LC522'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC523'>A corresponding label can be found by searching with the vim star command (*).</div><div class='line' id='LC524'>All labels can be found with a global search like :g/If0Label_/ or</div><div class='line' id='LC525'>:g/If0Label_\d\+/. All corresponding lines can be deleted with :g/If0Label_/d .</div><div class='line' id='LC526'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC527'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC528'>REMOVE THE ENCLOSING #if 0 ... #endif -CONSTRUCT.</div><div class='line' id='LC529'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC530'>The menu item &#39;remove #if #endif&#39; removes such a construct if the cursor is</div><div class='line' id='LC531'>in the middle of such a section or on one of the two enclosing lines. Nested</div><div class='line' id='LC532'>constructs will be untouched.</div><div class='line' id='LC533'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC534'>1.3.4  EX-COMMANDS                                          *csupport-prep-ex*</div><div class='line' id='LC535'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC536'>There are 4 additional Ex command which can be used to insert include</div><div class='line' id='LC537'>statements:</div><div class='line' id='LC538'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC539'>&nbsp;Ex command             hotkey     includes</div><div class='line' id='LC540'>&nbsp;-------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC541'>&nbsp;:IncludeStdLibrary     \ps        C standard library</div><div class='line' id='LC542'>&nbsp;:IncludeC99Library     \pc        C99 library</div><div class='line' id='LC543'>&nbsp;:IncludeCppLibrary     \+ps       C++ standard library</div><div class='line' id='LC544'>&nbsp;:IncludeCppCLibrary    \+pc       C standard library ( #include &lt;c...&gt; )</div><div class='line' id='LC545'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC546'>Type :Inc&lt;Tab&gt; and choose one of the commands. Now type an additional space</div><div class='line' id='LC547'>and a &lt;Tab&gt; to show the whole list list or type a space and a few leading</div><div class='line' id='LC548'>characters to reduce this list.</div><div class='line' id='LC549'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC550'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC551'>1.4  MENU &#39;Idioms&#39;                                           *csupport-idioms*</div><div class='line' id='LC552'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC553'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC554'>1.4.1  Item &#39;function&#39;                              *csupport-idioms-function*</div><div class='line' id='LC555'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC556'>NORMAL MODE, INSERT MODE:</div><div class='line' id='LC557'>The name of the function is asked for and the following lines (for function</div><div class='line' id='LC558'>name &quot;f&quot;) will be inserted:</div><div class='line' id='LC559'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC560'>&nbsp;&nbsp;void</div><div class='line' id='LC561'>&nbsp;&nbsp;f (  )</div><div class='line' id='LC562'>&nbsp;&nbsp;{</div><div class='line' id='LC563'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return ;</div><div class='line' id='LC564'>&nbsp;&nbsp;}        /* ----------  end of function f  ---------- */</div><div class='line' id='LC565'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC566'>VISUAL MODE:</div><div class='line' id='LC567'>Main or [static] function: the highlighted lines will go inside the new</div><div class='line' id='LC568'>function or main.</div><div class='line' id='LC569'>for-loops: the highlighted lines will be set in braces.</div><div class='line' id='LC570'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC571'>1.4.2  for-loop control                             *csupport-idioms-for-loop*</div><div class='line' id='LC572'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC573'>The menu items &#39;for( x=0; ... )&#39; and &#39;for( x=n-1; ... )&#39; can be used to write</div><div class='line' id='LC574'>the control statement for a for-loop counting upward or downward. These items</div><div class='line' id='LC575'>start an input dialog</div><div class='line' id='LC576'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC577'>&nbsp;[TYPE (expand)] VARIABLE [START [END [INCR.]]] :</div><div class='line' id='LC578'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC579'>asking for at least the name of the loop variable. The other parameters are</div><div class='line' id='LC580'>optional. The type is restricted to the following integral data types:</div><div class='line' id='LC581'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC582'>&nbsp;&nbsp;char</div><div class='line' id='LC583'>&nbsp;&nbsp;int</div><div class='line' id='LC584'>&nbsp;&nbsp;long</div><div class='line' id='LC585'>&nbsp;&nbsp;long int</div><div class='line' id='LC586'>&nbsp;&nbsp;long long</div><div class='line' id='LC587'>&nbsp;&nbsp;long long int</div><div class='line' id='LC588'>&nbsp;&nbsp;short</div><div class='line' id='LC589'>&nbsp;&nbsp;short int</div><div class='line' id='LC590'>&nbsp;&nbsp;size_t</div><div class='line' id='LC591'>&nbsp;&nbsp;unsigned </div><div class='line' id='LC592'>&nbsp;&nbsp;unsigned char</div><div class='line' id='LC593'>&nbsp;&nbsp;unsigned int</div><div class='line' id='LC594'>&nbsp;&nbsp;unsigned long</div><div class='line' id='LC595'>&nbsp;&nbsp;unsigned long int</div><div class='line' id='LC596'>&nbsp;&nbsp;unsigned long long</div><div class='line' id='LC597'>&nbsp;&nbsp;unsigned long long int</div><div class='line' id='LC598'>&nbsp;&nbsp;unsigned short</div><div class='line' id='LC599'>&nbsp;&nbsp;unsigned short int</div><div class='line' id='LC600'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC601'>One of these types can be specified by typing it completely or by typing zero</div><div class='line' id='LC602'>or more characters of its name and completing them to the full name by using</div><div class='line' id='LC603'>the tab key (tab completion). If the start of the type name is ambiguous (e.g.</div><div class='line' id='LC604'>&#39;uns&#39;) a list of completion candidates is provided to choose from.</div><div class='line' id='LC605'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC606'>1.4.3  Item &#39;open input file&#39;                          *csupport-idioms-input*</div><div class='line' id='LC607'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC608'>The item &#39;open input file&#39; will create the statements to open and close an</div><div class='line' id='LC609'>input file (e.g. with the file pointer &#39;infile&#39;).</div><div class='line' id='LC610'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC611'>1.4.4  Item &#39;open output file&#39;                        *csupport-idioms-output*</div><div class='line' id='LC612'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC613'>The item &#39;open output file&#39; will create the statements to open and close an</div><div class='line' id='LC614'>output file (e.g. with the file pointer &#39;outfile&#39;).</div><div class='line' id='LC615'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC616'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC617'>1.5  MENU &#39;Snippets&#39;                                       *csupport-snippets*</div><div class='line' id='LC618'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC619'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC620'>1.5.1  CODE SNIPPETS</div><div class='line' id='LC621'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC622'>Code snippets are pieces of code which are kept in separate files in a special</div><div class='line' id='LC623'>directory (e.g. a few lines of code or a complete template for a Makefile).</div><div class='line' id='LC624'>File names are used to identify the snippets.  The snippet directory will be</div><div class='line' id='LC625'>created during the installation  ( $HOME/.vim/codesnippets-c is the default).</div><div class='line' id='LC626'>Snippets are managed with the 3 items</div><div class='line' id='LC627'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC628'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;C/C++ -&gt; Snippets -&gt; read  code snippet</div><div class='line' id='LC629'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;C/C++ -&gt; Snippets -&gt; write code snippet</div><div class='line' id='LC630'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;C/C++ -&gt; Snippets -&gt; edit  code snippet</div><div class='line' id='LC631'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC632'>from the Snippets submenu.</div><div class='line' id='LC633'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC634'>CREATING A NEW SNIPPET</div><div class='line' id='LC635'>When nothing is marked, &quot;write code snippet&quot; will write the whole buffer</div><div class='line' id='LC636'>to a snippet file, otherwise the marked area will be written to a file.</div><div class='line' id='LC637'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC638'>INSERT A SNIPPET</div><div class='line' id='LC639'>Select the appropriate file from the snippet directory (&quot;read  code snippet&quot;).</div><div class='line' id='LC640'>The inserted lines will be indented.</div><div class='line' id='LC641'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC642'>EDIT A SNIPPET</div><div class='line' id='LC643'>This is a normal edit.</div><div class='line' id='LC644'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC645'>INDENTATION / NO INDENTATION</div><div class='line' id='LC646'>Code snippets are normally indented after insertion. To suppress indentation</div><div class='line' id='LC647'>add the file extension &quot;ni&quot; or &quot;noindent&quot; to the snippet file name, e.g.</div><div class='line' id='LC648'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC649'>&nbsp;&nbsp;parameter_handling.c.noindent</div><div class='line' id='LC650'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC651'>Snippet browser</div><div class='line' id='LC652'>---------------</div><div class='line' id='LC653'>Under a GUI a file requester will be put up. Without GUI the filename will be</div><div class='line' id='LC654'>read from the command line. You can change this behavior by setting a global</div><div class='line' id='LC655'>variable in your ~/.vimrc :</div><div class='line' id='LC656'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC657'>&nbsp;let g:C_GuiSnippetBrowser = &#39;commandline&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC658'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC659'>The default value is &#39;gui&#39;. </div><div class='line' id='LC660'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC661'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC662'>1.5.2   PICKING UP PROTOTYPES                                 *csupport-proto*</div><div class='line' id='LC663'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC664'>PICK UP FUNCTION PROTOTYPES (key mappings \np, \nf).</div><div class='line' id='LC665'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC666'>To make a prototype from a function head mark the function head and choose</div><div class='line' id='LC667'>&#39;Snippets -&gt; pick up funct. prototype&#39;. From the first six lines of</div><div class='line' id='LC668'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC669'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;void</div><div class='line' id='LC670'>&nbsp;&nbsp;print_double_array (  double array[],  /* array to print                */</div><div class='line' id='LC671'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;int    n,        /* number of elements to print   */</div><div class='line' id='LC672'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;int    columns,  /* number of elements per column */</div><div class='line' id='LC673'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;char*  arrayname /* array name                    */</div><div class='line' id='LC674'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;)</div><div class='line' id='LC675'>&nbsp;&nbsp;{</div><div class='line' id='LC676'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;...</div><div class='line' id='LC677'>&nbsp;&nbsp;}       /* ----------  end of function print_double_array  ---------- */</div><div class='line' id='LC678'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC679'>the prototype</div><div class='line' id='LC680'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC681'>&nbsp;&nbsp;void print_double_array ( double array[], int n, int columns, char* arrayname );</div><div class='line' id='LC682'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC683'>is produced and put in an internal buffer.</div><div class='line' id='LC684'>- Leading and trailing whitespaces are removed.</div><div class='line' id='LC685'>- All inner whitespaces are squeezed.</div><div class='line' id='LC686'>- All comments will be discarded.</div><div class='line' id='LC687'>- Trailing parts of the function body (e.g a &#39;{&#39; ) will also be removed.</div><div class='line' id='LC688'>- The class name and the scope resolution operator will be removed (C++ method</div><div class='line' id='LC689'>&nbsp;&nbsp;implementations).</div><div class='line' id='LC690'>Further prototypes can be picked up and gathered in the buffer.</div><div class='line' id='LC691'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC692'>PICK UP METHOD PROTOTYPES (key mapping \nm).</div><div class='line' id='LC693'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC694'>For C++ methods the menu item &#39;Snippets -&gt; pick up method prototype&#39; should be</div><div class='line' id='LC695'>used.  Namespace names and class names will be removed (exception: &#39;std::&#39; ).</div><div class='line' id='LC696'>The first two lines of</div><div class='line' id='LC697'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC698'>&nbsp;&nbsp;std::string</div><div class='line' id='LC699'>&nbsp;&nbsp;ROBOT::Robot::get_name  ( void )</div><div class='line' id='LC700'>&nbsp;&nbsp;{</div><div class='line' id='LC701'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return type_name;</div><div class='line' id='LC702'>&nbsp;&nbsp;}   /* -----  end of method Robot::get_name  ----- */</div><div class='line' id='LC703'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC704'>result in the prototype</div><div class='line' id='LC705'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC706'>&nbsp;&nbsp;std::string get_name ( void );</div><div class='line' id='LC707'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC708'>The 3 lines </div><div class='line' id='LC709'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC710'>&nbsp;&nbsp;template &lt;class T&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC711'>&nbsp;&nbsp;const Stack&lt;T&gt;&amp;</div><div class='line' id='LC712'>&nbsp;&nbsp;Stack&lt;T&gt;::operator = ( const Stack &amp;other )</div><div class='line' id='LC713'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC714'>result in the prototype</div><div class='line' id='LC715'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC716'>&nbsp;&nbsp;const Stack&amp; operator = ( const Stack &amp;other );</div><div class='line' id='LC717'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC718'>Folding may help picking up prototypes (see |csupport-folding|).</div><div class='line' id='LC719'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC720'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC721'>INSERT PROTOTYPES</div><div class='line' id='LC722'>With &#39;Snippets -&gt; insert prototype(s)&#39; all picked up prototypes currently in</div><div class='line' id='LC723'>the buffer will be inserted below the cursor.</div><div class='line' id='LC724'>The prototype buffer will be cleared after insertion.</div><div class='line' id='LC725'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC726'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC727'>DISCARD PROTOTYPES</div><div class='line' id='LC728'>The prototype buffer can be cleared with &#39;Snippets -&gt; clear prototype(s)&#39; .</div><div class='line' id='LC729'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC730'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC731'>SHOW PROTOTYPES</div><div class='line' id='LC732'>The list of gathered prototypes can be shown with</div><div class='line' id='LC733'>&#39;Snippets -&gt; show prototype(s)&#39;. The number and the filename are shown, e.g.</div><div class='line' id='LC734'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC735'>&nbsp;&nbsp;(1) matrix.c #  double** calloc_double_matrix ( int rows, int columns );</div><div class='line' id='LC736'>&nbsp;&nbsp;(2) matrix.c #  void free_double_matrix ( double **m );</div><div class='line' id='LC737'>&nbsp;&nbsp;(3) foomain.c #  void foo ( );</div><div class='line' id='LC738'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC739'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC740'>REMARK. Generating prototypes this way is nice in a small project. You may</div><div class='line' id='LC741'>want to use an extractor like cextract or something else.</div><div class='line' id='LC742'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC743'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC744'>1.5.3  Code Templates                                *csupport-templates-menu*</div><div class='line' id='LC745'>---------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC746'>Nearly all menu entries insert code snippets or comments. All these stuff is</div><div class='line' id='LC747'>taken from template files and can be changed by the user to meet his</div><div class='line' id='LC748'>requirements (see|csupport-templates|on how to use the template system).</div><div class='line' id='LC749'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC750'>The menu item &#39;edit local templates&#39; opens the main template file in a local</div><div class='line' id='LC751'>plugin installation. This is usually the file</div><div class='line' id='LC752'>&#39;~/.vim/c-support/templates/Templates&#39;.  There may be dependent files</div><div class='line' id='LC753'>loaded from the main file.  Now change whatever file you want, save it, and</div><div class='line' id='LC754'>click on the menu item &#39;reread templates&#39; to read in the file(s) and to</div><div class='line' id='LC755'>rebuild the internal representation of the templates.</div><div class='line' id='LC756'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC757'>The menu item &#39;edit global templates&#39; opens the main template file in a</div><div class='line' id='LC758'>system-wide plugin installation (see |csupport-system-wide|). This is</div><div class='line' id='LC759'>usually the file &#39;$VIM./vimfiles/c-support/templates/Templates&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC760'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC761'>Template browser</div><div class='line' id='LC762'>----------------</div><div class='line' id='LC763'>Under a GUI a file requester will be put up. Without GUI the filename will be</div><div class='line' id='LC764'>read from the command line. You can change this behavior by setting a global</div><div class='line' id='LC765'>variable in your ~/.vimrc :</div><div class='line' id='LC766'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC767'>&nbsp;let g:C_GuiTemplateBrowser = &#39;explorer&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC768'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC769'>The default value is &#39;gui&#39;. &#39;explorer&#39; will start the file explorer</div><div class='line' id='LC770'>(see help|:Explore|). To use the commandline asign &#39;commandline&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC771'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC772'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC773'>1.6  MENU &#39;C++&#39;                                                 *csupport-c++*</div><div class='line' id='LC774'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC775'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC776'>1.6.1  NORMAL MODE, INSERT MODE.                    *csupport-c++-normal-mode*</div><div class='line' id='LC777'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC778'>An empty statement will be inserted and in some cases properly indented. The</div><div class='line' id='LC779'>item &#39;try .. catch&#39; will insert the following lines:</div><div class='line' id='LC780'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC781'>&nbsp;&nbsp;try {</div><div class='line' id='LC782'>&nbsp;&nbsp;}</div><div class='line' id='LC783'>&nbsp;&nbsp;catch ( const &amp;ExceptObj ) {    // handle exception:</div><div class='line' id='LC784'>&nbsp;&nbsp;}</div><div class='line' id='LC785'>&nbsp;&nbsp;catch (...) {   // handle exception: unspecified</div><div class='line' id='LC786'>&nbsp;&nbsp;}</div><div class='line' id='LC787'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC788'>The cursor will go into the try block.</div><div class='line' id='LC789'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC790'>1.6.2  VISUAL MODE.                                 *csupport-c++-visual-mode*</div><div class='line' id='LC791'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC792'>The highlighted area can be surrounded by one of the following statements:</div><div class='line' id='LC793'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC794'>&nbsp;&nbsp;try - catch</div><div class='line' id='LC795'>&nbsp;&nbsp;catch</div><div class='line' id='LC796'>&nbsp;&nbsp;catch(...)</div><div class='line' id='LC797'>&nbsp;&nbsp;namespace { }</div><div class='line' id='LC798'>&nbsp;&nbsp;extern &quot;C&quot; { }</div><div class='line' id='LC799'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC800'>The whole statement will be indented after insertion.</div><div class='line' id='LC801'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC802'>1.6.3   METHOD IMPLEMENTATION                       *csupport-c++-method-impl*</div><div class='line' id='LC803'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC804'>The menu item &#39;method implement.&#39; asks for a method name. If this item is</div><div class='line' id='LC805'>called the first time you will see just an scope resolution operator.  If you</div><div class='line' id='LC806'>specify the scope this is used the next time you call this item.  If you use</div><div class='line' id='LC807'>one of the menu items to generate a class (see |csupport-templates|) the</div><div class='line' id='LC808'>scope will be extracted and used for the next method.</div><div class='line' id='LC809'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC810'>1.6.4  EX COMMANDS                                           *csupport-c++-ex*</div><div class='line' id='LC811'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC812'>There are 4 additional Ex command which can be used to insert include</div><div class='line' id='LC813'>statements. Please see |csupport-prep-ex|.</div><div class='line' id='LC814'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC815'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC816'>1.7  MENU &#39;Run&#39;                                                 *csupport-run*</div><div class='line' id='LC817'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC818'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC819'>1.7.1  MINIMAL MAKE FUNCTIONALITY                        *csupport-run-buffer*</div><div class='line' id='LC820'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC821'>The &#39;Run&#39; menu provides a minimal make functionality for single file projects</div><div class='line' id='LC822'>(e.g. in education) :</div><div class='line' id='LC823'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC824'>SAVE AND COMPILE</div><div class='line' id='LC825'>&#39;save and compile&#39; saves the buffer and run the compiler with the given</div><div class='line' id='LC826'>options (see |csupport-custom-glob-vars|).</div><div class='line' id='LC827'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC828'>An error window will be opened if the compiler reports errors and/or warnings.</div><div class='line' id='LC829'>Quickfix commands can now be used to jump to an error location.</div><div class='line' id='LC830'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC831'>Consider using maps like</div><div class='line' id='LC832'>&nbsp;&nbsp;map  &lt;silent&gt; &lt;F7&gt;    &lt;Esc&gt;:cprevious&lt;CR&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC833'>&nbsp;&nbsp;map  &lt;silent&gt; &lt;F8&gt;    &lt;Esc&gt;:cnext&lt;CR&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC834'>in your ~/.vimrc file to jump over the error locations and make navigation</div><div class='line' id='LC835'>easier.  The error list and the error locations in your source buffer will be</div><div class='line' id='LC836'>synchronized.</div><div class='line' id='LC837'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC838'>The filename extension for an object file can be set in ~.vimrc :</div><div class='line' id='LC839'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC840'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_ObjExtension = &#39;.obj&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC841'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC842'>The default is &#39;.o&#39; (&#39;.obj&#39; for Windows).</div><div class='line' id='LC843'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC844'>LINK</div><div class='line' id='LC845'>&#39;link&#39; makes an executable from the current buffer. If the buffer is not</div><div class='line' id='LC846'>saved, or no object is available or the object is older then the source step</div><div class='line' id='LC847'>&#39;save and compile&#39; is executed first.</div><div class='line' id='LC848'>The linkging will only be tried if the current buffer contains a main</div><div class='line' id='LC849'>function.</div><div class='line' id='LC850'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC851'>The behavior of the compiler / linker is determined by the options assigned to</div><div class='line' id='LC852'>the variables described in |csupport-custom-glob-vars| (4.group).</div><div class='line' id='LC853'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC854'>RUN</div><div class='line' id='LC855'>&#39;run&#39; runs the executable with the same name  as the current buffer. If the</div><div class='line' id='LC856'>buffer is not saved, or no executable is available or the executable is older</div><div class='line' id='LC857'>then the source steps &#39;save and compile&#39; and &#39;link&#39; are executed first.</div><div class='line' id='LC858'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC859'>The filename extension for an executable can be set in ~.vimrc :</div><div class='line' id='LC860'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC861'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_ExeExtension = &#39;.exe&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC862'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC863'>The default is the empty string.</div><div class='line' id='LC864'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC865'>1.7.2  COMMAND LINE ARGUMENTS                      *csupport-run-cmdline-args*</div><div class='line' id='LC866'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC867'>The item &#39;command line arguments&#39; calls an input dialog which asks for command</div><div class='line' id='LC868'>line arguments. These arguments are forwarded to the program which is run by</div><div class='line' id='LC869'>the &#39;run&#39; item. The arguments are kept until you change them.</div><div class='line' id='LC870'>For the first and only the first argument file name expansion will work (use</div><div class='line' id='LC871'>the Tab-key). Only the first string of the input can be expanded due to a</div><div class='line' id='LC872'>restriction of the Vim input function. To expand two or more filenames</div><div class='line' id='LC873'>specify them in reverse order: type the first characters of the last filename</div><div class='line' id='LC874'>and expand them. Go to the start of the input and type the beginning of the</div><div class='line' id='LC875'>last but one filename and expand it.</div><div class='line' id='LC876'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC877'>The arguments belong to the current buffer (that is, each buffer can have its</div><div class='line' id='LC878'>own arguments).</div><div class='line' id='LC879'>If the buffer gets a new name with &quot;save as&quot; the arguments will now belong to</div><div class='line' id='LC880'>the buffer with the new name.</div><div class='line' id='LC881'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC882'>The command line arguments can be followed by pipes and redirections:</div><div class='line' id='LC883'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC884'>&nbsp;&nbsp;11 22 | sort -rn | head -10 &gt; out</div><div class='line' id='LC885'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC886'>Caveat: If you look for the current arguments by calling this menu item again</div><div class='line' id='LC887'>be sure to leave it with a CR (not Esc !). Due to a limitation of an internal</div><div class='line' id='LC888'>Vim function CR will keep the arguments, Esc will discard them.</div><div class='line' id='LC889'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC890'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC891'>1.7.3  RUN make                                            *csupport-run-make*</div><div class='line' id='LC892'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC893'>The item &#39;make&#39; runs the external make program.  An error window will be</div><div class='line' id='LC894'>opened if the compiler or linker reports errors or warnings during the make</div><div class='line' id='LC895'>process.  Quickfix commands can now be used to jump to an error location.</div><div class='line' id='LC896'>Make looks for a makefile in the current directory (but see below).</div><div class='line' id='LC897'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC898'>When inside a makefile the hotkeys \rm, \rmc, \rcm,  and \rma are working (see</div><div class='line' id='LC899'>|csupport-usage-vim|).</div><div class='line' id='LC900'>The snippets collection contains a sample makefile which can easily adepted</div><div class='line' id='LC901'>for small projcts.</div><div class='line' id='LC902'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC903'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC904'>1.7.4  Choose Makefile                              *csupport-choose-makefile*</div><div class='line' id='LC905'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC906'>The menu item &#39;choose makefile&#39; let you specify a makefile in another</div><div class='line' id='LC907'>directory than the current one. Now this makefile will be used instead of the</div><div class='line' id='LC908'>one in the current directory (if any). Make is started from the directory in</div><div class='line' id='LC909'>which the makefile is contained. The working directory for the current buffer</div><div class='line' id='LC910'>will not be changed.</div><div class='line' id='LC911'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC912'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC913'>1.7.5  EXECUTABLE TO RUN                               *csupport-run-make-run*</div><div class='line' id='LC914'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC915'>The item &#39;executable to run&#39; asks for the name of the executable built by</div><div class='line' id='LC916'>make.  If the name given is nonempty this executable will be run by the menu</div><div class='line' id='LC917'>item &#39;run&#39; (\rr, C-F9).</div><div class='line' id='LC918'>To return to the default behavior (see |csupport-run-buffer|) remove the name</div><div class='line' id='LC919'>with the another &#39;executable to run&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC920'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC921'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC922'>1.7.6  RUN make clean                                *csupport-run-make-clean*</div><div class='line' id='LC923'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC924'>The item &#39;make&#39; runs the external make program with the standard target</div><div class='line' id='LC925'>&#39;clean&#39;.  If an alternate makefile has been chosen</div><div class='line' id='LC926'>(see|csupport-choose-makefile|), this one will be run from the directory in</div><div class='line' id='LC927'>which the makefile is contained.</div><div class='line' id='LC928'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC929'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC930'>1.7.7  COMMAND LINE ARGUMENTS FOR make                *csupport-run-make-args*</div><div class='line' id='LC931'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC932'>The item &#39;command line arguments for make&#39; calls an input dialog which asks</div><div class='line' id='LC933'>for command line arguments for make. These arguments are forwarded to make</div><div class='line' id='LC934'>when called by the menu item &#39;make&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC935'>For the first and only the first argument the file name expansion will work</div><div class='line' id='LC936'>(use the Tab-key).</div><div class='line' id='LC937'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC938'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC939'>1.7.8  SPLINT                                            *csupport-run-splint*</div><div class='line' id='LC940'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC941'>Splint is a tool for statically checking C programs (see http://www.splint.org).</div><div class='line' id='LC942'>Of course it has to be installed in order to be used within Vim.  The menu</div><div class='line' id='LC943'>item &#39;Run-&gt;splint&#39; will run the current buffer through splint.</div><div class='line' id='LC944'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC945'>An error window will be opened if splint has something to complain about.</div><div class='line' id='LC946'>Quickfix commands can now be used to jump to an error location.  For easier</div><div class='line' id='LC947'>navigation see tip under &#39;SAVE AND COMPILE&#39; |csupport-run-buffer|.</div><div class='line' id='LC948'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC949'>Splint has many options. Presumably the best way is to keep the options in an</div><div class='line' id='LC950'>option file (~/.splintrc). For a quick try you can use the menu item</div><div class='line' id='LC951'>&#39;Run-&gt;cmd. line arg. for splint&#39; to specify some buffer related options.</div><div class='line' id='LC952'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC953'>When vim is started this plugin will check whether splint is executable.
