If</div><div class='line' id='LC954'>not, the menu item will *NOT&#39; be visible.</div><div class='line' id='LC955'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC956'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC957'>1.7.9  CODECHECK                                      *csupport-run-codecheck*</div><div class='line' id='LC958'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC959'>CodeCheck (TM) is a commercial code analyzing tool produced by Abraxas</div><div class='line' id='LC960'>Software, Inc.  (www.abraxas-software.com).</div><div class='line' id='LC961'>Of course it has to be installed in order to be used within Vim.  The menu</div><div class='line' id='LC962'>item &#39;Run-&gt;CodeCheck&#39; will run the current buffer through CodeCheck.</div><div class='line' id='LC963'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC964'>An error window will be opened if CodeCheck has something to complain about.</div><div class='line' id='LC965'>Quickfix commands can now be used to jump to an error location.  For easier</div><div class='line' id='LC966'>navigation see tip under &#39;SAVE AND COMPILE&#39; |csupport-run-buffer|.</div><div class='line' id='LC967'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC968'>CodeCheck has many options.  For a quick try you can use the menu item</div><div class='line' id='LC969'>&#39;Run-&gt;cmd. line arg. for CodeCheck&#39; to specify some buffer related options.</div><div class='line' id='LC970'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC971'>CodeCheck will be run with default options (see |csupport-custom-glob-vars|).</div><div class='line' id='LC972'>The default options can be overwritten by  placing a global variable in</div><div class='line' id='LC973'>~/.vimrc , e.g.</div><div class='line' id='LC974'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC975'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let  g:C_CodeCheckOptions = &quot;-K13 -Rmeyers&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC976'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC977'>The default name for the executable is &#39;check&#39;.  There are other names in use</div><div class='line' id='LC978'>on different platforms.  The name can be changed by placing a global variable</div><div class='line' id='LC979'>in ~/.vimrc , e.g.</div><div class='line' id='LC980'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC981'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let  g:C_CodeCheckExeName = &quot;chknt.exe&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC982'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC983'>When vim is started this plugin will check whether CodeCheck is executable. If</div><div class='line' id='LC984'>not, the menu item will *NOT&#39; be visible.</div><div class='line' id='LC985'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC986'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC987'>1.7.10  INDENT                                           *csupport-run-indent*</div><div class='line' id='LC988'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC989'>The formatter &#39;indent&#39; can be run over the whole buffer.  Before formatting a</div><div class='line' id='LC990'>buffer this buffer will be saved to disk and you will be asked for a</div><div class='line' id='LC991'>confirmation.</div><div class='line' id='LC992'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC993'>Indent has many options. These are kept in the file &#39;.indent.pro&#39; in your home</div><div class='line' id='LC994'>directory. See the indent manual for more information.</div><div class='line' id='LC995'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC996'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC997'>1.7.11  HARDCOPY                                       *csupport-run-hardcopy*</div><div class='line' id='LC998'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC999'>Generates a PostScript file from the whole buffer or from a marked region.</div><div class='line' id='LC1000'>On a Windows system a printer dialog is displayed.</div><div class='line' id='LC1001'>The hardcopy goes to the current working directory.  If the buffer contains</div><div class='line' id='LC1002'>documentation or other material from non-writable directories the hardcopy</div><div class='line' id='LC1003'>goes to the HOME directory. The output destination will be shown in a message.</div><div class='line' id='LC1004'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1005'>The print header contains date and time for the current locale. The definition</div><div class='line' id='LC1006'>used is</div><div class='line' id='LC1007'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1008'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let s:C_Printheader = &quot;%&lt;%f%h%m%&lt;  %=%{strftime(&#39;%x %X&#39;)}     Page %N&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC1009'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1010'>The current locale can be overwritten by changing the language, e.g.</div><div class='line' id='LC1011'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1012'>&nbsp;&nbsp;:language C</div><div class='line' id='LC1013'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1014'>or by setting a global variable in the file ~/.vimrc , e.g. :</div><div class='line' id='LC1015'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1016'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_Printheader = &quot;%&lt;%f%h%m%&lt;  %=%{strftime(&#39;%x %X&#39;)}     SEITE %N&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC1017'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1018'>See :h printheader and :h strftime()  for more details.</div><div class='line' id='LC1019'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1020'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1021'>1.7.12  REBUILD TEMPLATES                             *csupport-run-templates*</div><div class='line' id='LC1022'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1023'>After editing one or more template files  a click on this item rereads the</div><div class='line' id='LC1024'>template files and rebuilds all templates.</div><div class='line' id='LC1025'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1026'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1027'>1.7.13  XTERM SIZE                                        *csupport-run-xterm*</div><div class='line' id='LC1028'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1029'>The size of the xterm used for  running a program (below) can be set by this</div><div class='line' id='LC1030'>menu item. The default is 80 columns with 24 lines.</div><div class='line' id='LC1031'>This feature is not available under Windows.</div><div class='line' id='LC1032'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1033'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1034'>1.7.14  OUTPUT REDIRECTION                               *csupport-run-output*</div><div class='line' id='LC1035'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1036'>Running a program can be done in one of three ways:</div><div class='line' id='LC1037'>(1) Run the program from the gVim command line.</div><div class='line' id='LC1038'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This is for interactive programs with little input and output.</div><div class='line' id='LC1039'>(2) Run the program and direct the output into a window with name &quot;C-Output&quot;.</div><div class='line' id='LC1040'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The buffer and its content will disappear when the window is closed and</div><div class='line' id='LC1041'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;reused otherwise.</div><div class='line' id='LC1042'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This is for non-interactive programs with little to very much output.</div><div class='line' id='LC1043'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;You have unlimited line length, regex search, navigation, ...</div><div class='line' id='LC1044'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The tabstop value will be set to 8  for &quot;C-Output&quot;.</div><div class='line' id='LC1045'>(3) Run the program in an xterm.</div><div class='line' id='LC1046'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1047'>The output method can be chosen from the menu item &#39;Run-&gt;output: ...&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC1048'>This menu has three states:</div><div class='line' id='LC1049'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1050'>&nbsp;&nbsp;output: VIM-&gt;buffer-&gt;xterm</div><div class='line' id='LC1051'>&nbsp;&nbsp;output: BUFFER-&gt;xterm-&gt;vim</div><div class='line' id='LC1052'>&nbsp;&nbsp;output: XTERM-&gt;vim-&gt;buffer</div><div class='line' id='LC1053'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1054'>The first (uppercase) item shows the current method.  The default is &#39;vim&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC1055'>This can be changed by setting the variable g:C_OutputGvim to another value.</div><div class='line' id='LC1056'>Possible values are &#39;vim&#39;, &#39;buffer&#39; and &#39;xterm&#39; .</div><div class='line' id='LC1057'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1058'>The xterm defaults can be set in ~/.vimrc by the variable g:C_XtermDefaults .</div><div class='line' id='LC1059'>The default is &quot;-fa courier -fs 12 -geometry 80x24&quot; :</div><div class='line' id='LC1060'>&nbsp;&nbsp;font name     : -fa courier</div><div class='line' id='LC1061'>&nbsp;&nbsp;font size     : -fs 12</div><div class='line' id='LC1062'>&nbsp;&nbsp;terminal size : -geometry 80x24</div><div class='line' id='LC1063'>See &#39;xterm -help&#39; for more options. Xterms are not available under Windows.</div><div class='line' id='LC1064'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1065'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1066'>1.8  &#39;help&#39;                                                    *csupport-help*</div><div class='line' id='LC1067'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1068'>Plugin help</div><div class='line' id='LC1069'>-----------</div><div class='line' id='LC1070'>The root menu item &#39;help (plugin)&#39; shows this plugin help in a help window.</div><div class='line' id='LC1071'>The help tags must have been generated with</div><div class='line' id='LC1072'>&nbsp;&nbsp;:helptags ~/.vim/doc</div><div class='line' id='LC1073'>The hotkey is \hp (for &quot;help plugin&quot;).</div><div class='line' id='LC1074'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1075'>Displaying a manual</div><div class='line' id='LC1076'>-------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1077'>The root menu item &#39;show manual&#39; shows the manual for the word under the</div><div class='line' id='LC1078'>cursor. If there is more than one manual a selection list will be presented.</div><div class='line' id='LC1079'>If there is no word under the cursor you can type in a name.  An interface to</div><div class='line' id='LC1080'>the on-line reference manuals must be installed (usually man(1) for</div><div class='line' id='LC1081'>Linux/Unix, see|csupport-custom-glob-vars|).</div><div class='line' id='LC1082'>The hotkey is \hm (for &quot;help manual&quot;).</div><div class='line' id='LC1083'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1084'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1085'>2.  USAGE WITHOUT GUI  (Vim)                              *csupport-usage-vim*</div><div class='line' id='LC1086'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1087'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1088'>The frequently used constructs can be inserted with key mappings.  The</div><div class='line' id='LC1089'>mappings are also described in the document c-hot-keys.pdf (reference card,</div><div class='line' id='LC1090'>part of this package).</div><div class='line' id='LC1091'>Hint: Typing speed matters. The combination of a leader (&#39;\&#39;) and the</div><div class='line' id='LC1092'>following character(s) will only be recognized for a short time.</div><div class='line' id='LC1093'>Some mappings can be used with range (of lines). In normal mode</div><div class='line' id='LC1094'>&nbsp;&nbsp;\cl</div><div class='line' id='LC1095'>appends a end-of-line comment to the current line,  whereas </div><div class='line' id='LC1096'>&nbsp;&nbsp;4\cl</div><div class='line' id='LC1097'>appends end-of-line comments to the 4 lines starting with the current line.</div><div class='line' id='LC1098'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1099'>Legend:  (i) insert mode, (n) normal mode, (v) visual mode</div><div class='line' id='LC1100'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;[n] range</div><div class='line' id='LC1101'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1102'>&nbsp;&nbsp;-- Help ---------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1103'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1104'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\hm       show manual for word under the cursor (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1105'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\hp       show plugin help                      (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1106'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1107'>&nbsp;&nbsp;-- Comments -----------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1108'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1109'>&nbsp;&nbsp;[n]\cl       end-of-line comment                 (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1110'>&nbsp;&nbsp;[n]\cj       adjust end-of-line comment(s)       (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1111'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\cs       set end-of-line comment column      (n)</div><div class='line' id='LC1112'>&nbsp;&nbsp;[n]\c*       code -&gt; comment /* */               (n,v)</div><div class='line' id='LC1113'>&nbsp;&nbsp;[n]\cc       code -&gt; comment //                  (n,v)</div><div class='line' id='LC1114'>&nbsp;&nbsp;[n]\co       comment -&gt; code                     (n,v)</div><div class='line' id='LC1115'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\cfr      frame comment                       (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1116'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\cfu      function comment                    (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1117'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\cme      method description                  (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1118'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ccl      class description                   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1119'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\cfdi     file description (implementation)   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1120'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\cfdh     file description (header)           (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1121'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ccs      C/C++-file section  (tab. compl.)   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1122'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\chs      H-file section      (tab. compl.)   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1123'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ckc      keyword comment     (tab. compl.)   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1124'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\csc      special comment     (tab. compl.)   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1125'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\cd       date                                (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1126'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ct       date \&amp; time                        (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1127'>&nbsp;&nbsp;[n]\cx       toggle comments: C &lt;--&gt; C++         (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1128'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1129'>&nbsp;&nbsp;-- Statements ---------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1130'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1131'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\sd       do { } while                        (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1132'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\sf       for                                 (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1133'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\sfo      for { }                             (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1134'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\si       if                                  (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1135'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\sif      if { }                              (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1136'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\sie      if else                             (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1137'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\sife     if { } else { }                     (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1138'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\se       else { }                            (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1139'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\sw       while                               (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1140'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\swh      while { }                           (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1141'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ss       switch                              (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1142'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\sc       case                                (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1143'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\s{ \sb   { }                                 (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1144'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1145'>&nbsp;&nbsp;-- Preprocessor -------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1146'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1147'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ps       choose a standard library include   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1148'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pc       choose a C99 include                (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1149'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\p&lt;       #include &lt;&gt;                         (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1150'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\p&quot;       #include &quot;&quot;                         (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1151'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pd       #define                             (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1152'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pu       #undef                              (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1153'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pif      #if  #endif                         (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1154'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pie      #if  #else #endif                   (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1155'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pid      #ifdef #else #endif                 (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1156'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pin      #ifndef #else #endif                (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1157'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pind     #ifndef #def #endif                 (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1158'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pi0      #if 0 #endif                        (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1159'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pr0      remove #if 0 #endif                 (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1160'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pe       #error                              (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1161'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pl       #line                               (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1162'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\pp       #pragma                             (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1163'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1164'>&nbsp;&nbsp;-- Idioms -------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1165'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1166'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\if       function                            (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1167'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\isf      static function                     (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1168'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\im       main()                              (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1169'>&nbsp;&nbsp;[n]\i0       for( x=0; x&lt;n; x+=1 )               (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1170'>&nbsp;&nbsp;[n]\in       for( x=n-1; x&gt;=0; x-=1 )            (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1171'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ie       enum   + typedef                    (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1172'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\is       struct + typedef                    (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1173'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\iu       union  + typedef                    (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1174'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ip       printf()                            (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1175'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\isc      scanf()                             (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1176'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ica      p=calloc()                          (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1177'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ima      p=malloc()                          (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1178'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ire      p=realloc()                         (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1179'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\isi      sizeof()                            (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1180'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ias      assert()                            (n,v)</div><div class='line' id='LC1181'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ii       open input file                     (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1182'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\io       open output file                    (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1183'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ifs      fscanf                              (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1184'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ifp      fprintf                             (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1185'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1186'>&nbsp;&nbsp;-- Snippets -----------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1187'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1188'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\nr       read code snippet                   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1189'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\nw       write code snippet                  (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1190'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ne       edit code snippet                   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1191'>&nbsp;&nbsp;[n]\nf       pick up function prototype          (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1192'>&nbsp;&nbsp;[n]\np       pick up function prototype          (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1193'>&nbsp;&nbsp;[n]\nm       pick up method prototype            (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1194'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ni       insert prototype(s)                 (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1195'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\nc       clear  prototype(s)                 (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1196'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ns       show   prototype(s)                 (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1197'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ntl      edit local templates                (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1198'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ntg      edit global templates               (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1199'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ntr      rebuild templates                   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1200'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1201'>&nbsp;&nbsp;-- C++ ----------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1202'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1203'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+co      cout  &lt;&lt;  &lt;&lt; endl;                  (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1204'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+&quot;       &lt;&lt; &quot;&quot;                               (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1205'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+c       class                               (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1206'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+ps      #include &lt;...&gt; STL                  (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1207'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+pc      #include &lt;c..&gt; C                    (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1208'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+cn      class (using new)                   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1209'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+ci      class implementation                (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1210'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+cni     class (using new) implementation    (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1211'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+mi      method implementation               (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1212'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+ai      accessor implementation             (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1213'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1214'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+tc      template class                      (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1215'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+tcn     template class (using new)          (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1216'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+tci     template class implementation       (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1217'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+tcni    template class (using new) impl.    (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1218'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+tmi     template method implementation      (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1219'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+tai     template accessor implementation    (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1220'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1221'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+tf      template function                   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1222'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+ec      error class                         (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1223'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+tr      try ... catch                       (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1224'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+ca      catch                               (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1225'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\+c.      catch(...)                          (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1226'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1227'>&nbsp;&nbsp;-- Run ----------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1228'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1229'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rc       save and compile                    (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1230'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rl       link                                (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1231'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rr       run                                 (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1232'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ra       set comand line arguments           (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1233'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rm       run make                            (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1234'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rmc      run &#39;make clean&#39;                    (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1235'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rcm      choose makefile                     (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1236'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rme      executable to run                   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1237'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rma      cmd. line arg. for make             (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1238'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rp       run splint                          (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1239'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rpa      cmd. line arg. for splint           (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1240'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rk       run CodeCheck (TM)                  (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1241'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rka      cmd. line arg. for CodeCheck (TM)   (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1242'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rd       run indent                          (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1243'>&nbsp;[n]\rh       hardcopy buffer                     (n,v,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1244'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rs       show plugin settings                (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1245'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\rx       set xterm size                      (n, only Linux/UNIX &amp; GUI)</div><div class='line' id='LC1246'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\ro       change output destination           (n,i)</div><div class='line' id='LC1247'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1248'>The hotkeys are defined in the file type plugin c.vim (part of this csupport</div><div class='line' id='LC1249'>plugin package) and described in the document c-hot-keys.pdf</div><div class='line' id='LC1250'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1251'>Changing the default map leader &#39;\&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1252'>-----------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1253'>The map leader can be changed by the user by setting a global variable in the</div><div class='line' id='LC1254'>file .vimrc </div><div class='line' id='LC1255'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1256'>&nbsp;let g:C_MapLeader  = &#39;,&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1257'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1258'>The map leader is now a comma. The &#39;line end comment&#39; command is now defined</div><div class='line' id='LC1259'>as &#39;,cl&#39;. This setting will be used as a so called local leader and influences</div><div class='line' id='LC1260'>only files with filetype &#39;c&#39; and &#39;cpp&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC1261'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1262'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1263'>3.  HOTKEYS                                                 *csupport-hotkeys*</div><div class='line' id='LC1264'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1265'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1266'>The following hotkeys are defined in normal, visual and insert mode:</div><div class='line' id='LC1267'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1268'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;F9   compile and link</div><div class='line' id='LC1269'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Alt-F9   write buffer and compile</div><div class='line' id='LC1270'>&nbsp;&nbsp;Ctrl-F9   run executable</div><div class='line' id='LC1271'>&nbsp;Shift-F9   set command line arguments</div><div class='line' id='LC1272'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1273'>&nbsp;Shift-F2   switch between source files and header files</div><div class='line' id='LC1274'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1275'>The hotkeys are defined in the file type plugin  c.vim.  All hotkeys from the</div><div class='line' id='LC1276'>non-GUI mode also work for gVim (see |csupport-usage-vim|).</div><div class='line' id='LC1277'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1278'>Shift-F2 can be used to switch between source files and header files if the</div><div class='line' id='LC1279'>plugin a.vim (http://vim.sourceforge.net/scripts/script.php?script_id=31) is</div><div class='line' id='LC1280'>present.  To suppress the creation of a new header file when switching from a</div><div class='line' id='LC1281'>source file the file ~/.vimrc should contain a line</div><div class='line' id='LC1282'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1283'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:alternateNoDefaultAlternate = 1</div><div class='line' id='LC1284'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1285'>A header file will only be opened if it already exists.</div><div class='line' id='LC1286'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1287'>The Shift-key is dead when you are working with Vim in a console terminal</div><div class='line' id='LC1288'>(non-Gui). You could add </div><div class='line' id='LC1289'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1290'>&nbsp;&nbsp;noremap   \a        :A&lt;CR&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1291'>&nbsp;inoremap   \a   &lt;C-C&gt;:A&lt;CR&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1292'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1293'>to get a hot key for this case.</div><div class='line' id='LC1294'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1295'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1296'>4.  CUSTOMIZATION                                            *csupport-custom*</div><div class='line' id='LC1297'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1298'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1299'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1300'>4.1  GLOBAL VARIABLES                              *csupport-custom-glob-vars*</div><div class='line' id='LC1301'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div              &#39;on&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1312'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1313'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_CodeSnippets           plugin_dir.&#39;/c-support/codesnippets/&#39;</div><div id='LC1316'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_MenuHeader             &#39;yes&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1317'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_OutputGvim             &#39;vim&#39;</div><div class='line' 80x24&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1320'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_Printheader            &quot;%&lt;%f%h%m%&lt;  %=%{strftime(&#39;%x %X&#39;)}     Page %N&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC1323'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_GuiTemplateBrowser     &#39;gui&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1324'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1325'>&nbsp;&nbsp;Linux/UNIX:</div><div class='line'     &#39;.obj&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1333'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_ExeExtension          &#39;.exe&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1334'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_CCompiler             &#39;gcc.exe&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1335'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_CplusCompiler         &#39;g++.exe&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1336'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_Man                   &#39;man.exe&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1337'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_VimCompilerName        gcc</div><div class='line' id='LC1338'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_CFlags                 &#39;-Wall -g -O0 -c&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1339'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_LFlags                 &#39;-Wall -g -O0&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1340'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_Libs                   &#39;-lm&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1341'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_LineEndCommColDefault  49</div><div class='line' id='LC1342'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_CExtension             &#39;c&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1343'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_TypeOfH                &#39;cpp&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1344'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_SourceCodeExtensions   &#39;c cc cp cxx cpp CPP c++ C i ii&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1345'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1346'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_CodeCheckExeName       &#39;check&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1347'>&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_CodeCheckOptions       &#39;-K13&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1348'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1349'>The variable plugin_dir will automatically be set to one of the following values:</div><div class='line' id='LC1350'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$HOME.&#39;/.vim/&#39;        for Linux/Unix</div><div class='line' id='LC1351'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$VIM.&#39;/vimfiles/&#39;     for Windows</div><div class='line' class='line' id='LC1355'>&nbsp;1. group: g:C_GlobalTemplateFile : Sets the master template file (see|csupport-templates|)</div><div class='line' id='LC1356'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_LocalTemplateFile  : Sets the local template file  (see|csupport-templates|)</div><div class='line' |csupport-snippets|).</div><div class='line' id='LC1362'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_Dictionary_File    : The name(s) of the dictionary file(s) used completion (see also |csupport-dictionary|)</div><div class='line' id='LC1364'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_LoadMenus          : Load menus and mappings (&quot;yes&quot;, &quot;no&quot;) at startup.</div><div class='line' id='LC1365'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_MenuHeader         : Switch the submenu header on/off.</div><div class='line' id='LC1366'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_OutputGvim         : when program is running output goes to the vim</div><div class='line' id='LC1367'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;command line (&quot;vim&quot;), to a buffer (&quot;buffer&quot;) or to</div><div class='line' id='LC1368'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;an xterm (&quot;xterm&quot;).</div><div class='line' id='LC1369'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_Root               : The name of the root menu entry of this plugin</div><div class='line' id='LC1370'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(see |csupport-custom-root|).</div><div class='line' id='LC1371'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_XtermDefaults      : the xterm defaults</div><div class='line' id='LC1373'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_MapLeader          : the map leader for hotkeys (see|csupport-usage-vim|)</div><div class='line' id='LC1374'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_GuiSnippetBrowser  : code snippet browser: &#39;gui&#39;, &#39;commandline&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1375'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_GuiTemplateBrowser : code template browser: &#39;gui&#39;, &#39;explorer&#39;, &#39;commandline&#39; </div><div class='line' id='LC1376'>&nbsp;</div><div class='line' id='LC1377'>&nbsp;3. group: g:C_CExtension             : Extension of C files. Everything else is C++.</div><div class='line' id='LC1378'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_TypeOfH                : filetype of header files with extension &#39;h&#39; (c,cpp)</div><div class='line' id='LC1379'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_SourceCodeExtensions   : filename extensions for C/C++</div><div class='line' id='LC1380'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;implementation files</div><div class='line' id='LC1381'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_CCompiler              : The name of the C compiler.</div><div class='line' id='LC1384'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_Man                    : The name of the man utility.</div><div class='line' id='LC1385'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_CFlags                 : Compiler flags used for a compilation.</div><div class='line' id='LC1386'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_LFlags                 : Compiler flags used for linkage.</div><div class='line' id='LC1387'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_Libs                   : Libraries to link with.</div><div class='line' id='LC1388'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_ObjExtension           : C/C+ file extension for objects</div><div class='line' id='LC1389'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(leading point required if not empty)</div><div class='line' id='LC1390'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_ExeExtension           : C/C+ file extension for executables</div><div class='line' id='LC1391'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(leading point required if not empty)</div><div class='line' id='LC1392'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_LineEndCommColDefault  : Default starting column for end-of-line comments.</div><div class='line' id='LC1393'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_CodeCheckExeName       : The name of the CodeCheck (TM) executable</div><div class='line' id='LC1394'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(the default is &#39;check&#39;)</div><div class='line' id='LC1395'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;g:C_CodeCheckOptions       : Default options for CodeCheck (TM)</div><div class='line' id='LC1396'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(see |csupport-run-codecheck|).</div><div class='line' id='LC1397'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1398'>To override the default add appropriate assignments to ~/.vimrc .</div><div class='line' id='LC1399'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1400'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1401'>4.2  THE ROOT MENU                                      *csupport-custom-root*</div><div class='line' id='LC1402'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1403'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1404'>The variable g:C_Root, if set (in &#39;.vimrc&#39; or in &#39;.gvimrc&#39;), gives the name</div><div class='line' id='LC1405'>of the single gVim root menu entry in which the C/C++ submenus will be put.</div><div class='line' id='LC1406'>The default is</div><div class='line' id='LC1407'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1408'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&#39;&amp;C\/C\+\+.&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1409'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#39;&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1410'>Note the terminating dot. </div><div class='line' id='LC1411'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1412'>If you want to set the plugin root menu into another menu, e.g. &#39;Plugin&#39;,</div><div class='line' id='LC1413'>this is done by the following line in &#39;.vimrc&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1414'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1415'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_Root = &#39;&amp;Plugin.&amp;C\/C\+\+.&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1416'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1417'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1418'>4.3  SYSTEM-WIDE INSTALLATION                           *csupport-system-wide*</div><div class='line' id='LC1419'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1420'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1421'>A system-wide installation (one installation for all users) is done as</div><div class='line' id='LC1422'>follows.</div><div class='line' id='LC1423'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1424'>As *** SUPERUSER *** :</div><div class='line' id='LC1425'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1426'>(1) Find the Vim installation directory.</div><div class='line' id='LC1427'>The Vim Ex command &#39;:echo $VIM&#39; gives &#39;/usr/local/share/vim&#39; or something like</div><div class='line' id='LC1428'>that. Beyond this directory you will find the Vim installation,  e.g. in</div><div class='line' id='LC1429'>&#39;/usr/local/share/vim/vim73&#39; if Vim version 7.3 has been installed</div><div class='line' id='LC1430'>(Windows: &#39;C:\Program Files\Vim&#39;).</div><div class='line' id='LC1431'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1432'>(2) Create a new subdirectory &#39;vimfiles&#39;, e.g. &#39;/usr/local/share/vim/vimfiles&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1433'>(Windows: &#39;C:\Program Files\Vim\vimfiles&#39;).</div><div class='line' id='LC1434'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1435'>(3) Install C/C++ Support</div><div class='line' id='LC1436'>Copy the archive cvim.zip to this new directory and unpack it:</div><div class='line' id='LC1437'>&nbsp;&nbsp;unzip cvim.zip</div><div class='line' id='LC1438'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1439'>(4) Generate the help tags:</div><div class='line' id='LC1440'>&nbsp;&nbsp;:helptags $VIM/vimfiles/doc</div><div class='line' id='LC1441'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1442'>SPECIAL CASES. Some Linux distributions use non-standard names for Vim</div><div class='line' id='LC1443'>directories. SUSE has a directory &#39;/usr/share/vim/site&#39; to put plugins in.</div><div class='line' id='LC1444'>These directories will not be found automatically.  After installing the</div><div class='line' id='LC1445'>plugin below &#39;/usr/share/vim/site&#39; the use of the templates will be enabled by</div><div class='line' id='LC1446'>the following line in &#39;~/.vimrc&#39;:</div><div class='line' id='LC1447'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1448'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_GlobalTemplateFile = &#39;/usr/share/vim/site/c-support/templates/Templates&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1449'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1450'>As *** USER *** :</div><div class='line' id='LC1451'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1452'>Create your private snippet directory:</div><div class='line' id='LC1453'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1454'>&nbsp;&nbsp;mkdir --parents  ~/.vim/c-support/codesnippets</div><div class='line' id='LC1455'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1456'>You may want to copy the snippets coming with this plugin (in</div><div class='line' id='LC1457'>$VIM/vimfiles/c-support/codesnippets) into the new directory or to set a</div><div class='line' id='LC1458'>link to the global directory.</div><div class='line' id='LC1459'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1460'>Create your private template directory:</div><div class='line' id='LC1461'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1462'>&nbsp;&nbsp;mkdir --parents  ~/.vim/c-support/templates</div><div class='line' id='LC1463'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1464'>Create a private template file &#39;Templates&#39; (compulsory) in this directory to</div><div class='line' id='LC1465'>overwrite some macros, e.g.</div><div class='line' id='LC1466'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1467'>&nbsp;*|AUTHOR|*    = your name</div><div class='line' id='LC1468'>&nbsp;*|AUTHORREF|* = ...</div><div class='line' id='LC1469'>&nbsp;*|EMAIL|*     = ...</div><div class='line' id='LC1470'>&nbsp;*|COMPANY|*   = ...</div><div class='line' id='LC1471'>&nbsp;*|COPYRIGHT|* = ...</div><div class='line' id='LC1472'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1473'>You can also have local templates which overwrite the global ones. To suppress</div><div class='line' id='LC1474'>the messages in this case set a global variable in &#39;~/.vimrc&#39; (Windows:</div><div class='line' id='LC1475'>&#39;~\_vimrc&#39;) :</div><div class='line' id='LC1476'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1477'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_TemplateOverwrittenMsg= &#39;no&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1478'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1479'>The default is &#39;yes&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC1480'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1481'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1482'>5.  TEMPLATE FILES AND TAGS                               *csupport-templates*</div><div class='line' id='LC1483'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1484'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1485'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1486'>5.1  TEMPLATE FILES                                 *csupport-templates-files*</div><div class='line' id='LC1487'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1488'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1489'>Nearly all menu entries insert code snippets or comments. All of these are</div><div class='line' id='LC1490'>contained within template files and can be changed by the user to meet their</div><div class='line' id='LC1491'>requirements.</div><div class='line' id='LC1492'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1493'>The master template file is &#39;$HOME/.vim/c-support/templates/Templates&#39; for a</div><div class='line' id='LC1494'>user installation and  &#39;$VIM/vimfiles/c-support/templates/Templates&#39; for a</div><div class='line' id='LC1495'>system-wide installation (see|csupport-system-wide|).</div><div class='line' id='LC1496'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1497'>The master template file starts with a macro section followed by templates for</div><div class='line' id='LC1498'>single menu items or better by including other template files grouping the</div><div class='line' id='LC1499'>templates according to the menu structure of this plugin. The master file</div><div class='line' id='LC1500'>could look like this:</div><div class='line' id='LC1501'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1502'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$</div><div class='line' id='LC1503'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$ =============================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1504'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$ ========== USER MACROS ======================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1505'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$ =============================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1506'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$</div><div class='line' id='LC1507'>&nbsp;*|AUTHOR|*    = Dr. Fritz Mehner</div><div class='line' id='LC1508'>&nbsp;*|AUTHORREF|* = mn</div><div class='line' id='LC1509'>&nbsp;*|EMAIL|*     = mehner@fh-swf.de</div><div class='line' id='LC1510'>&nbsp;*|COMPANY|*   = FH SÃ¼dwestfalen, Iserlohn</div><div class='line' id='LC1511'>&nbsp;*|COPYRIGHT|* = Copyright (c)*|YEAR|,|AUTHOR|*</div><div class='line' id='LC1512'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$</div><div class='line' id='LC1513'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$ =============================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1514'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$ ========== FILE INCLUDES ====================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1515'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$ =============================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1516'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$</div><div class='line' id='LC1517'>&nbsp;*|includefile|* = c.comments.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1518'>&nbsp;*|includefile|* = c.cpp.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1519'>&nbsp;*|includefile|* = c.idioms.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1520'>&nbsp;*|includefile|* = c.preprocessor.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1521'>&nbsp;*|includefile|* = c.statements.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1522'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1523'>Lines starting with a dollar sign are comments. The section starting</div><div class='line' id='LC1524'>with *|AUTHOR|* assigns values to predefined tags</div><div class='line' id='LC1525'>(see|csupport-templates-macros|) to personalize some templates. Other</div><div class='line' id='LC1526'>predefined tags with given default values can be used (e.g. *|YEAR|* ).</div><div class='line' id='LC1527'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1528'>User defined tags are possible. They have the following syntax:</div><div class='line' id='LC1529'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1530'>&nbsp;*|macroname|* = replacement</div><div class='line' id='LC1531'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1532'>A macroname starts with a letter (uppercase or lowercase) followed by zero or</div><div class='line' id='LC1533'>more letters, digits or underscores.</div><div class='line' id='LC1534'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1535'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1536'>5.2  MACROS                                        *csupport-templates-macros*</div><div class='line' id='LC1537'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1538'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1539'>The following macro names are predefined. The first group is used to</div><div class='line' id='LC1540'>personalize templates.</div><div class='line' id='LC1541'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1542'>&nbsp;----------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1543'>&nbsp;PREDEFINED MACROS  DEFAULT VALUE</div><div class='line' id='LC1544'>&nbsp;----------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1545'>*|AUTHOR|*          &quot;&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC1546'>*|AUTHORREF|*       &quot;&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC1547'>*|EMAIL|*           &quot;&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC1548'>*|COMPANY|*         &quot;&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC1549'>*|PROJECT|*         &quot;&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC1550'>*|COPYRIGHTHOLDER|* &quot;&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC1551'>*|STYLE|*           &quot;&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC1552'>*|includefile|*     &quot;&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC1553'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1554'>*|BASENAME|*        filename without path and suffix</div><div class='line' id='LC1555'>*|DATE|*            the preferred date representation for the current locale</div><div class='line' id='LC1556'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;without the time</div><div class='line' id='LC1557'>*|FILENAME|*        filename without path</div><div class='line' id='LC1558'>*|PATH|*            path without filename</div><div class='line' id='LC1559'>*|SUFFIX|*          filename suffix</div><div class='line' id='LC1560'>*|TIME|*            the preferred time representation for the current locale</div><div class='line' id='LC1561'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;without the date and the time zone or name or abbreviation</div><div class='line' id='LC1562'>*|YEAR|*            the year as a decimal number including the century</div><div class='line' id='LC1563'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1564'>The macro *|includefile|* can  be used to include an additional template file.</div><div class='line' id='LC1565'>A file will be included only once. Commenting and uncommenting include macros</div><div class='line' id='LC1566'>is a simple way to switch between several sets of templates (see also</div><div class='line' id='LC1567'>|csupport-run-templates|). Overwriting existing macros and templates is</div><div class='line' id='LC1568'>possible.</div><div class='line' id='LC1569'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1570'>&nbsp;----------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1571'>&nbsp;PREDEFINED TAGS</div><div class='line' id='LC1572'>&nbsp;----------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1573'>&nbsp;&lt;CURSOR&gt;,{CURSOR}    The cursor position after insertion of a template</div><div class='line' id='LC1574'>&nbsp;&lt;+text+&gt;,&lt;-text-&gt;,   Jump targets in templates. Jump with Ctrl-j.</div><div class='line' id='LC1575'>&nbsp;{+text+},{-text-}    See |csupport-templates-jump|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1576'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1577'>&nbsp;&lt;SPLIT&gt;              The split point when inserting in visual mode</div><div class='line' id='LC1578'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(see|csupport-templates-definition|)</div><div class='line' id='LC1579'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1580'>A dependent template file can start with its own macro section. There is no</div><div class='line' id='LC1581'>need to have all user defined macros in the master file.</div><div class='line' id='LC1582'>When the first template definition is found (see below) macro definitions are</div><div class='line' id='LC1583'>no longer recognized.</div><div class='line' id='LC1584'>Use the tag variant with curly braces if the indentation of the following line</div><div class='line' id='LC1585'>is wrong after template insertion.</div><div class='line' id='LC1586'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1587'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1588'>5.2.1  USER DEFINED FORMATS FOR DATE AND TIME        *csupport-templates-date*</div><div class='line' id='LC1589'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1590'>The format for *|DATE|* ,*|TIME|* , and*|YEAR|* can be set by the user. The</div><div class='line' id='LC1591'>defaults are</div><div class='line' id='LC1592'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*|DATE|*        &#39;%x&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1593'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*|TIME|*        &#39;%X&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1594'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*|YEAR|*        &#39;%Y&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1595'>See the manual page of the C function strftime() for the format.  The accepted</div><div class='line' id='LC1596'>format depends on your system, thus this is not portable!  The maximum length</div><div class='line' id='LC1597'>of the result is 80 characters.</div><div class='line' id='LC1598'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1599'>User defined formats can be set using the following global variables in</div><div class='line' id='LC1600'>~/.vimrc ,  e.g.</div><div class='line' id='LC1601'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_FormatDate            = &#39;%D&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1602'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_FormatTime            = &#39;%H:%M&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1603'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_FormatYear            = &#39;year %Y&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1604'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1605'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1606'>5.3  TEMPLATES                                      *csupport-templates-names*</div><div class='line' id='LC1607'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1608'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1609'>5.3.1  Template names</div><div class='line' id='LC1610'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1611'>The template behind a menu entry is identified by a given name. The first part</div><div class='line' id='LC1612'>of the name identifies the menu, the second part identifies the item. The</div><div class='line' id='LC1613'>modes are also hard coded (see|csupport-templates-definition|for the use of</div><div class='line' id='LC1614'>&lt;SPLIT&gt;).</div><div class='line' id='LC1615'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1616'>&nbsp;&nbsp;TEMPLATE NAME                                              MODES</div><div class='line' id='LC1617'>&nbsp;--------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1618'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1619'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.class                                              normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1620'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.end-of-line-comment                                normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1621'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-description                                   normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1622'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-description-header                            normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1623'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-cpp-class-defs                        normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1624'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-cpp-class-implementations-exported    normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1625'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-cpp-class-implementations-local       normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1626'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-cpp-data-types                        normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1627'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-cpp-function-defs-exported            normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1628'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-cpp-function-defs-local               normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1629'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-cpp-header-includes                   normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1630'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-cpp-local-variables                   normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1631'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-cpp-macros                          normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1634'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-hpp-exported-class-defs               normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1635'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-hpp-exported-data-types               normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1636'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-hpp-exported-function-declarations    normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1637'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-hpp-exported-typedefs                 normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1638'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-hpp-exported-variables                normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1639'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.file-section-hpp-header-includes                          normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1642'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.function                                           normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1643'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.keyword-bug                                        normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1644'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.keyword-compiler                          normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1647'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.keyword-tricky                                     normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1648'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.keyword-warning                                    normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1649'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.keyword-workaround                                 normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1650'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.method                                             normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1651'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.special-constant-type-is-long                      normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1652'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.special-constant-type-is-unsigned-long             normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1653'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.special-constant-type-is-unsigned                  normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1654'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.special-empty                                      normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1655'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.special-fall-through                               normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1656'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.special-implicit-type-conversion                   normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1657'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.special-no-return                                  normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1658'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.special-not-reached                                normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1659'>&nbsp;&nbsp;comment.special-remains-to-be-implemented                  normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1660'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1661'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.accessor-implementation                                normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1662'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.catch
