                                         normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1665'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.class-definition                                       normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1666'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.class-implementation                                   normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1667'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.class-using-new-definition                             normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1668'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.class-using-new-implementation                         normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1669'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.cout-operator                                          normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1670'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.cout                                                   normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1671'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.error-class                                            normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1672'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.extern                                                 normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1673'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.method-implementation                                  normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1674'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.namespace-block                                        normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1675'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.namespace                                              normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1676'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.namespace-std                                          normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1677'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.open-input-file                                        normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1678'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.open-output-file                                       normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1679'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.operator-in                                            normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1680'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.operator-out                                           normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1681'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-boolalpha                           normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1682'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-dec                                 normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1683'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-endl                                normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1684'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-fixed                               normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1685'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-flush                               normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1686'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-hex                                 normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1687'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-internal                            normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1688'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-left                                normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1689'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-oct                                 normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1690'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-right                               normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1691'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-scientific                          normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1692'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-setbase                             normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1693'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-setfill                             normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1694'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-setiosflag                          normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1695'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-setprecision                        normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1696'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-setw                                normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1697'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-showbase                            normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1698'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-showpoint                           normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1699'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-showpos                             normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1700'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.output-manipulator-uppercase                           normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1701'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.rtti-const-cast                                        normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1702'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.rtti-dynamic-cast                                      normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1703'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.rtti-reinterpret-cast                                  normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1704'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.rtti-static-cast                                       normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1705'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.rtti-typeid                                            normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1706'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.template-accessor-implementation                       normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1707'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.template-class-definition                              normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1708'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.template-class-implementation                          normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1709'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.template-class-using-new-definition                    normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1710'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.template-class-using-new-implementation                normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1711'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.template-function                                      normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1712'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.template-method-implementation                         normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1713'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cpp.try-catch                                              normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1714'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1715'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.assert                                              normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1716'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.calloc                                              normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1717'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.enum                                                normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1718'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.fprintf                                             normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1719'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.fscanf                                              normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1720'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.function                                            normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1721'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.function-static                                     normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1722'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.main                                                normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1723'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.malloc                                              normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1724'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.open-input-file                                     normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1725'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.open-output-file                                    normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1726'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.printf                                              normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1727'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.scanf                                               normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1728'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.sizeof                                              normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1729'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.struct                                              normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1730'>&nbsp;&nbsp;idioms.union                                               normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1731'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1732'>&nbsp;&nbsp;preprocessor.define                                        normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1733'>&nbsp;&nbsp;preprocessor.ifdef-else-endif                              normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1734'>&nbsp;&nbsp;preprocessor.if-else-endif                                 normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1735'>&nbsp;&nbsp;preprocessor.ifndef-def-endif                              normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1736'>&nbsp;&nbsp;preprocessor.ifndef-else-endif                             normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1737'>&nbsp;&nbsp;preprocessor.include-global                                normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1738'>&nbsp;&nbsp;preprocessor.include-local                                 normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1739'>&nbsp;&nbsp;preprocessor.undefine                                      normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1740'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1741'>&nbsp;&nbsp;statements.block                                           normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1742'>&nbsp;&nbsp;statements.case                                            normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1743'>&nbsp;&nbsp;statements.do-while                                        normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1744'>&nbsp;&nbsp;statements.for-block                                       normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1745'>&nbsp;&nbsp;statements.for                                             normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1746'>&nbsp;&nbsp;statements.if-block-else                                   normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1747'>&nbsp;&nbsp;statements.if-block                                        normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1748'>&nbsp;&nbsp;statements.if-else                                         normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1749'>&nbsp;&nbsp;statements.if                                              normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1750'>&nbsp;&nbsp;statements.switch                                          normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1751'>&nbsp;&nbsp;statements.while-block                                     normal, visual</div><div class='line' id='LC1752'>&nbsp;&nbsp;statements.while                                           normal</div><div class='line' id='LC1753'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1754'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1755'>5.3.2  Template definition                     *csupport-templates-definition*</div><div class='line' id='LC1756'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1757'>A template definition starts with a template head line with the following</div><div class='line' id='LC1758'>syntax:</div><div class='line' id='LC1759'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1760'>&nbsp;&nbsp;== templatename == [ position == ]</div><div class='line' id='LC1761'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1762'>The templatename is one of the above template identifiers. The position</div><div class='line' id='LC1763'>attribute is optional. Possible attribute values are:</div><div class='line' id='LC1764'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1765'>&nbsp;&nbsp;above     insert the template before the current line</div><div class='line' id='LC1766'>&nbsp;&nbsp;append    append the template to the current line</div><div class='line' id='LC1767'>&nbsp;&nbsp;below     insert the template below the current line</div><div class='line' id='LC1768'>&nbsp;&nbsp;insert    insert the template at the cursor position</div><div class='line' id='LC1769'>&nbsp;&nbsp;start     insert the template before the first line of the buffer</div><div class='line' id='LC1770'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1771'>An example:</div><div class='line' id='LC1772'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1773'>&nbsp;&nbsp;== comment.function ==</div><div class='line' id='LC1774'>&nbsp;&nbsp;/*</div><div class='line' id='LC1775'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* ===  FUNCTION  =======================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1776'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*         Name:  &lt;CURSOR&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1777'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*  Description:</div><div class='line' id='LC1778'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* ======================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1779'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*/</div><div class='line' id='LC1780'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1781'>The definition of a template ends at the next head line or at the end of the</div><div class='line' id='LC1782'>file.</div><div class='line' id='LC1783'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1784'>Templates for the visual mode can use &lt;SPLIT&gt;. The text before &lt;SPLIT&gt; will</div><div class='line' id='LC1785'>than be inserted above the marked area, the text after &lt;SPLIT&gt; will be</div><div class='line' id='LC1786'>inserted behind the marked area. An example:</div><div class='line' id='LC1787'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1788'>&nbsp;&nbsp;== statements.if-block-else ==</div><div class='line' id='LC1789'>&nbsp;&nbsp;if ( &lt;CURSOR&gt; ) {</div><div class='line' id='LC1790'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;SPLIT&gt;} else {</div><div class='line' id='LC1791'>&nbsp;&nbsp;}</div><div class='line' id='LC1792'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1793'>If applied to the marked block</div><div class='line' id='LC1794'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1795'>&nbsp;&nbsp;xxxxxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC1796'>&nbsp;&nbsp;xxxxxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC1797'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1798'>this template yields</div><div class='line' id='LC1799'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1800'>&nbsp;&nbsp;if (  ) {</div><div class='line' id='LC1801'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;xxxxxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC1802'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;xxxxxxxxxxx</div><div class='line' id='LC1803'>&nbsp;&nbsp;} else {</div><div class='line' id='LC1804'>&nbsp;&nbsp;}</div><div class='line' id='LC1805'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1806'>The templates with a visual mode are shown in the table under</div><div class='line' id='LC1807'>|csupport-templates-names|.</div><div class='line' id='LC1808'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1809'>5.3.3  Template expansion                       *csupport-templates-expansion*</div><div class='line' id='LC1810'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1811'>There are additional ways to control the expansion of a template.</div><div class='line' id='LC1812'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1813'>USER INPUT</div><div class='line' id='LC1814'>----------</div><div class='line' id='LC1815'>If the usage of a yet undefined user macro starts with a question mark the</div><div class='line' id='LC1816'>user will be asked for the replacement first, e.g. with the following template</div><div class='line' id='LC1817'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1818'>&nbsp;&nbsp;== idioms.function ==</div><div class='line' id='LC1819'>&nbsp;&nbsp;void&lt;CURSOR&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1820'>&nbsp;*|?FUNCTION_NAME|* (  )</div><div class='line' id='LC1821'>&nbsp;&nbsp;{</div><div class='line' id='LC1822'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;SPLIT&gt; return ;</div><div class='line' id='LC1823'>&nbsp;&nbsp;}   /* -----  end of function*|FUNCTION_NAME|* ----- */</div><div class='line' id='LC1824'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1825'>The user can specify the function name which then will be applied twice. If</div><div class='line' id='LC1826'>the macro was already in use the old value will be suggested as default.</div><div class='line' id='LC1827'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1828'>MACRO MANIPULATION</div><div class='line' id='LC1829'>------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1830'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1831'>A macro expansion can be controlled by the following attributes</div><div class='line' id='LC1832'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1833'>&nbsp;&nbsp;:l    change macro text to lowercase</div><div class='line' id='LC1834'>&nbsp;&nbsp;:u    change macro text to uppercase</div><div class='line' id='LC1835'>&nbsp;&nbsp;:c    capitalize macro text</div><div class='line' id='LC1836'>&nbsp;&nbsp;:L    legalize name</div><div class='line' id='LC1837'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1838'>The include guard template is an example for the use of &#39;:L&#39; :</div><div class='line' id='LC1839'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1840'>&nbsp;&nbsp;== preprocessor.ifndef-def-endif ==</div><div class='line' id='LC1841'>&nbsp;#ifndef *|?BASENAME:L|_INC*</div><div class='line' id='LC1842'>&nbsp;#define *|BASENAME|_INC*</div><div class='line' id='LC1843'>&nbsp;&lt;CURSOR&gt;&lt;SPLIT&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1844'>&nbsp;#endif   // ----- #ifndef*|BASENAME|_INC* -----</div><div class='line' id='LC1845'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1846'>The base name of the file shall be used as part of the include guard name.</div><div class='line' id='LC1847'>The predefined macro*|BASENAME|* is used to ask for this part because this</div><div class='line' id='LC1848'>macro has already a defined value. That value can accepted or replaced by the</div><div class='line' id='LC1849'>user. For the filename &#39;test test++test.h&#39; the legalized base name</div><div class='line' id='LC1850'>&#39;TEST_TEST_TEST&#39; will be suggested.</div><div class='line' id='LC1851'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1852'>Legalization means:</div><div class='line' id='LC1853'>&nbsp;- replace all whitespaces by underscores</div><div class='line' id='LC1854'>&nbsp;- replace all non-word characters by underscores</div><div class='line' id='LC1855'>&nbsp;- replace &#39;+&#39; and &#39;-&#39; by underscore</div><div class='line' id='LC1856'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1857'>5.3.4  The macros &lt;+text+&gt; etc.                      *csupport-templates-jump*</div><div class='line' id='LC1858'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1859'>There are four macro types which can be used as jump targets in templates:</div><div class='line' id='LC1860'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1861'>&nbsp;&lt;+text+&gt;   Can be jumped to by hitting Ctrl-j.</div><div class='line' id='LC1862'>&nbsp;{+text+}   Same as &lt;+text+&gt;. Used in cases where indentation gives unwanted</div><div class='line' id='LC1863'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;results with the first one.</div><div class='line' id='LC1864'>&nbsp;</div><div class='line' id='LC1865'>&nbsp;&lt;-text-&gt;   Same as the two above. Will be removed if the template is used</div><div class='line' id='LC1866'>&nbsp;{-text-}   in visual mode.</div><div class='line' id='LC1867'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1868'>The text inside the brackets is userdefined and can be empty. The text</div><div class='line' id='LC1869'>can be composed from letters (uppercase and lowercase), digits, underscores</div><div class='line' id='LC1870'>and blanks. After the insertion of an template these jump targets will be</div><div class='line' id='LC1871'>highlighted. </div><div class='line' id='LC1872'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1873'>5.3.5  Command Ctrl-j                                        *csupport-Ctrl-j*</div><div class='line' id='LC1874'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1875'>Use the command Ctrl-j to jump to the next target. The target will be removed</div><div class='line' id='LC1876'>and the mode will switched to insertion. Ctrl-j works in normal and in insert</div><div class='line' id='LC1877'>mode.</div><div class='line' id='LC1878'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1879'>The template for a function can be written as follows:</div><div class='line' id='LC1880'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1881'>&nbsp;== idioms.function ==</div><div class='line' id='LC1882'>&nbsp;void&lt;CURSOR&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC1883'>&nbsp;|?FUNCTION_NAME| ( &lt;+argument list+&gt; )</div><div class='line' id='LC1884'>&nbsp;{</div><div class='line' id='LC1885'>&nbsp;&lt;SPLIT&gt;  return &lt;+return value+&gt;;</div><div class='line' id='LC1886'>&nbsp;}    /* -----  end of function |FUNCTION_NAME|  ----- */</div><div class='line' id='LC1887'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1888'>The cursor will be set behind &#39;void&#39;. You can remove &#39;void&#39; easily with </div><div class='line' id='LC1889'>Ctrl-w (delete word before cursor) and insert a new type. A Ctrl-j leads you</div><div class='line' id='LC1890'>to the argument list. The target disappears and you can type on. When the</div><div class='line' id='LC1891'>function body is written a final Ctrl-j brings you to the return statement.</div><div class='line' id='LC1892'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1893'>The following example shows the usage of the type {-text-}. The idiom for the</div><div class='line' id='LC1894'>opening of a file marks the line before the file is closed. This is also the</div><div class='line' id='LC1895'>line where the template will be split to surround a marked area. In this case</div><div class='line' id='LC1896'>(visual mode) the target is not needed and therefore removed (minus signs as</div><div class='line' id='LC1897'>mnemonic). In normal and insert mode the target is meaningful and will be</div><div class='line' id='LC1898'>therefore be present.  The form &lt;-...-&gt; would result in a wrong indentation of</div><div class='line' id='LC1899'>the file close statement. The brace type will be handled as a block and the</div><div class='line' id='LC1900'>indentation will be correct.</div><div class='line' id='LC1901'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1902'>&nbsp;== cpp.open-input-file ==</div><div class='line' id='LC1903'>&nbsp;char *ifs_file_name = &quot;&lt;CURSOR&gt;&quot;;    /* input  file name       */</div><div class='line' id='LC1904'>&nbsp;ifstream ifs;              /* create ifstream object */</div><div class='line' id='LC1905'>&nbsp;</div><div class='line' id='LC1906'>&nbsp;ifs.open (ifs_file_name);    /* open ifstream          */</div><div class='line' id='LC1907'>&nbsp;if (!ifs) {</div><div class='line' id='LC1908'>&nbsp;&nbsp;cerr &lt;&lt; &quot;\nERROR : failed to open input  file &quot; &lt;&lt; ifs_file_name &lt;&lt; endl;</div><div class='line' id='LC1909'>&nbsp;&nbsp;exit (EXIT_FAILURE);</div><div class='line' id='LC1910'>&nbsp;}</div><div class='line' id='LC1911'>&nbsp;&lt;SPLIT&gt;{-continue here-}</div><div class='line' id='LC1912'>&nbsp;ifs.close ();    /* close ifstream         */</div><div class='line' id='LC1913'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1914'>Extra feature of Ctrl-j</div><div class='line' id='LC1915'>-----------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1916'>If none of the above described targets is left Ctrl-j can be used to jump</div><div class='line' id='LC1917'>behind closing brackets, parenthesis, braces,  or string terminators (&#39;&quot;`).</div><div class='line' id='LC1918'>This feature is limited to the current line. Ctrl-j does not jump behind the</div><div class='line' id='LC1919'>last character in a line.</div><div class='line' id='LC1920'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1921'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1922'>How to switch the mapping for Ctrl-j off</div><div class='line' id='LC1923'>----------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC1924'>The original meaning of Ctrl-j is &#39;move [n] lines downward&#39; (see |CTRL-j|).</div><div class='line' id='LC1925'>If you are accustomed to use the deafult and don&#39;t like these jump targets you</div><div class='line' id='LC1926'>can switch them off.  Put the following line in the file .vimrc :</div><div class='line' id='LC1927'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1928'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_Ctrl_j   = &#39;off&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC1929'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1930'>The default value of g:C_Ctrl_j is &#39;on&#39;. You do not have to change the</div><div class='line' id='LC1931'>template files. All jump targets will be removed before a template will be</div><div class='line' id='LC1932'>inserted. </div><div class='line' id='LC1933'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1934'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1935'>5.4  SWITCHING BETWEEN TEMPLATE SETS                 *csupport-templates-sets*</div><div class='line' id='LC1936'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1937'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1938'>This plugin comes with two sets of templates. These are suggestions. You may</div><div class='line' id='LC1939'>want to have additional sets for different projects or occasionally want to</div><div class='line' id='LC1940'>use doxygen style comments.  To facilitate switching use the macro*|STYLE|*</div><div class='line' id='LC1941'>(|csupport-templates-files|) to define a unique name and the</div><div class='line' id='LC1942'>IF-ENDIF-construct to choose a particular set of files for example:</div><div class='line' id='LC1943'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1944'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;...</div><div class='line' id='LC1945'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1946'>&nbsp;*|STYLE|*    = C</div><div class='line' id='LC1947'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$</div><div class='line' id='LC1948'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$ =============================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1949'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$ ========== FILE INCLUDES ====================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1950'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$ =============================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1951'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$</div><div class='line' id='LC1952'>&nbsp;&nbsp;== IF *|STYLE|* IS C  ==</div><div class='line' id='LC1953'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$</div><div class='line' id='LC1954'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|includefile| = c.comments.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1955'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|includefile| = c.cpp.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1956'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|includefile| = c.idioms.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1957'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|includefile| = c.preprocessor.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1958'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|includefile| = c.statements.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1959'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$</div><div class='line' id='LC1960'>&nbsp;&nbsp;== ENDIF ==</div><div class='line' id='LC1961'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1962'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;...</div><div class='line' id='LC1963'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1964'>The syntax is as follows:</div><div class='line' id='LC1965'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1966'>&nbsp;&nbsp;== IF macro_name IS macro_value  ==</div><div class='line' id='LC1967'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</div><div class='line' id='LC1968'>&nbsp;&nbsp;== ENDIF ==</div><div class='line' id='LC1969'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1970'>Includes outside an IF-ENDIF construct are associated with the default style</div><div class='line' id='LC1971'>&#39;default&#39;. A style set does not have to a complete set of templates. For an</div><div class='line' id='LC1972'>incomplete set the other templates are taken from the default style.</div><div class='line' id='LC1973'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1974'>IF, IS, and ENDIF are keywords.</div><div class='line' id='LC1975'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1976'>HINT. Use these constructs to avoid overwriting your templates when updating</div><div class='line' id='LC1977'>csupport. Copy and rename the set of files you want to change and surround the</div><div class='line' id='LC1978'>includes with an appropriate IF-construct:</div><div class='line' id='LC1979'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1980'>&nbsp;*|STYLE|*    = MY_C</div><div class='line' id='LC1981'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$</div><div class='line' id='LC1982'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;...</div><div class='line' id='LC1983'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$</div><div class='line' id='LC1984'>&nbsp;&nbsp;== IF *|STYLE|* IS MY_C  ==</div><div class='line' id='LC1985'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|includefile| = my_c.comments.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1986'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|includefile| = my_c.cpp.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1987'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|includefile| = my_c.idioms.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1988'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|includefile| = my_c.preprocessor.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1989'>&nbsp;&nbsp;|includefile| = my_c.statements.template</div><div class='line' id='LC1990'>&nbsp;&nbsp;== ENDIF ==</div><div class='line' id='LC1991'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1992'>Keep a copy of the main template file &#39;Templates&#39; because this file will be</div><div class='line' id='LC1993'>overwritten if you do not update manually.</div><div class='line' id='LC1994'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1995'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1996'>5.5  BINDING A STYLE TO A FILE EXTENSION             *csupport-templates-bind*</div><div class='line' id='LC1997'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC1998'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC1999'>You can bind the existing styles to one or more filename extensions. To do so</div><div class='line' id='LC2000'>assign a Dictionary to the global variable g:C_Styles in &#39;~/.vimrc&#39; :</div><div class='line' id='LC2001'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2002'>let g:C_Styles = { &#39;*.c,*.h&#39; : &#39;default&#39;, &#39;*.cc,*.cpp,*.hh&#39; : &#39;CPP&#39; }</div><div class='line' id='LC2003'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2004'>A Dictionary is created with a comma separated list of entries in curly</div><div class='line' id='LC2005'>braces.  Each entry has a key and a value, separated by a colon.  Each key can</div><div class='line' id='LC2006'>only appear once. The keys are themselves a comma separated list of filename</div><div class='line' id='LC2007'>pattern. The values are existing styles defined in the template files.</div><div class='line' id='LC2008'>The given style will be set automatically when switching to a buffer or</div><div class='line' id='LC2009'>opening a new buffer with the associated filename pattern and supersedes the</div><div class='line' id='LC2010'>macro *|STYLE|* .</div><div class='line' id='LC2011'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2012'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2013'>6.  C/C++ DICTIONARY                                     *csupport-dictionary*</div><div class='line' id='LC2014'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2015'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2016'>The files</div><div class='line' id='LC2017'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2018'>&nbsp;c-c++-keywords.list</div><div class='line' id='LC2019'>&nbsp;k+r.list</div><div class='line' id='LC2020'>&nbsp;stl_index.list</div><div class='line' id='LC2021'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2022'>are a part of this plugin and can be used (together with your own lists) as</div><div class='line' id='LC2023'>dictionaries for automatic word completion.  This feature is enabled by</div><div class='line' id='LC2024'>default. The default word lists are</div><div class='line' id='LC2025'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2026'>&nbsp;&nbsp;plugin_dir/c-support/wordlists/c-c++-keywords.list</div><div class='line' id='LC2027'>&nbsp;&nbsp;plugin_dir/c-support/wordlists/k+r.list</div><div class='line' id='LC2028'>&nbsp;&nbsp;plugin_dir/c-support/wordlists/stl_index.list</div><div class='line' id='LC2029'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2030'>The variable plugin_dir will automatically be set by the plugin to one of the</div><div class='line' id='LC2031'>following values:</div><div class='line' id='LC2032'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$HOME.&#39;/.vim/&#39;        for Linux/Unix</div><div class='line' id='LC2033'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$VIM.&#39;/vimfiles/&#39;     for Windows</div><div class='line' id='LC2034'>If you want to use an additional list MyC.list put the following lines into</div><div class='line' id='LC2035'>&nbsp;~/.vimrc :</div><div class='line' id='LC2036'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2037'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_Dictionary_File = PLUGIN_DIR.&#39;/c-support/wordlists/c-c++-keywords.list,&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC2038'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\                   PLUGIN_DIR.&#39;/c-support/wordlists/k+r.list,&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC2039'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\                   PLUGIN_DIR.&#39;/c-support/wordlists/stl_index.list,&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC2040'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\                   PLUGIN_DIR.&#39;/c-support/wordlists/MyC.list&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC2041'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2042'>When in file ~/.vimrc the name PLUGIN_DIR has to be replaced by $HOME or</div><div class='line' id='LC2043'>$VIM (see above). Whitespaces in the pathnames have to be escaped with a</div><div class='line' id='LC2044'>backslash.</div><div class='line' id='LC2045'>The right side is a comma separated list of files. Note the point at the end</div><div class='line' id='LC2046'>of the first line (string concatenation) and the backslash in front of the</div><div class='line' id='LC2047'>second line (continuation line).</div><div class='line' id='LC2048'>You can use Vim&#39;s dictionary feature CTRL-X, CTRL-K (and CTRL-P, CTRL-N).</div><div class='line' id='LC2049'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2050'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2051'>7.  EXTENDING  ctags                                          *csupport-ctags*</div><div class='line' id='LC2052'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2053'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2054'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC2055'>7.1  make AND qmake                                      *csupport-ctags-make*</div><div class='line' id='LC2056'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC2057'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2058'>The use of the Vim plugin taglist.vim (Author: Yegappan Lakshmanan) is highly</div><div class='line' id='LC2059'>recommended. It uses the program ctags which generates tag files for 3 dozen</div><div class='line' id='LC2060'>languages (Exuberant Ctags, Darren Hiebert, http://ctags.sourceforge.net).</div><div class='line' id='LC2061'>With the following extensions the list of targets in a makefile can be shown</div><div class='line' id='LC2062'>in the taglist window.</div><div class='line' id='LC2063'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2064'>&nbsp;1) Append the file customization.ctags to the file $HOME/.ctags .</div><div class='line' id='LC2065'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2066'>&nbsp;2) Add the following lines (from customization.vimrc) to $HOME/.vimrc :</div><div class='line' id='LC2067'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2068'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;</div><div class='line' id='LC2069'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;-------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC2070'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot; taglist.vim : toggle the taglist window</div><div class='line' id='LC2071'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot; taglist.vim : define the title texts for make</div><div class='line' id='LC2072'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot; taglist.vim : define the title texts for qmake</div><div class='line' id='LC2073'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;-------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC2074'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;noremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;F11&gt;  &lt;Esc&gt;&lt;Esc&gt;:Tlist&lt;CR&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC2075'>&nbsp;&nbsp;inoremap &lt;silent&gt; &lt;F11&gt;  &lt;Esc&gt;&lt;Esc&gt;:Tlist&lt;CR&gt;</div><div class='line' id='LC2076'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2077'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let tlist_make_settings  = &#39;make;m:makros;t:targets;i:includes&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC2078'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let tlist_qmake_settings = &#39;qmake;t:SystemVariables&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC2079'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2080'>&nbsp;&nbsp;if has(&quot;autocmd&quot;)</div><div class='line' id='LC2081'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot; ----------  qmake : set file type for *.pro  ----------</div><div class='line' id='LC2082'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;autocmd BufNewFile,BufRead *.pro  set filetype=qmake</div><div class='line' id='LC2083'>&nbsp;&nbsp;endif &quot; has(&quot;autocmd&quot;)</div><div class='line' id='LC2084'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2085'>&nbsp;3) restart vim/gvim</div><div class='line' id='LC2086'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2087'>The two maps will toggle the taglist window (hotkey F11) in all editing modes.</div><div class='line' id='LC2088'>The two assignments define the headings for the (q)make sections in the</div><div class='line' id='LC2089'>taglist window.  The autocmd set the file type &#39;qmake&#39; for the filename</div><div class='line' id='LC2090'>extension &#39;pro&#39; (ctags needs this).</div><div class='line' id='LC2091'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2092'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC2093'>7.2  TEMPLATES                                      *csupport-ctags-templates*</div><div class='line' id='LC2094'>------------------------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC2095'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2096'>If you frequently change the plugin  templates and you are using the taglist</div><div class='line' id='LC2097'>plugin (section above) you may want to use this plugin for navigation. This is</div><div class='line' id='LC2098'>achieved in two steps. First add a new language definition to  the file</div><div class='line' id='LC2099'>$HOME/.ctags :</div><div class='line' id='LC2100'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2101'>&nbsp;&nbsp;--langdef=template</div><div class='line' id='LC2102'>&nbsp;&nbsp;--langmap=template:.template,TEMPLATE</div><div class='line' id='LC2103'>&nbsp;&nbsp;--regex-template=/^==\s+([^=]+)\s+==\s*(\s+==\s+([^=]+)\s+==)?/\1/t,template/</div><div class='line' id='LC2104'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2105'>Now add the following lines to the file $HOME/.vimrc :</div><div class='line' id='LC2106'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2107'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let tlist_template_settings  = &#39;template;t:template&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC2108'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;---------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC2109'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot; plugin templates : set filetype for *.template  </div><div class='line' id='LC2110'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&quot;---------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC2111'>&nbsp;&nbsp;if has(&quot;autocmd&quot;)</div><div class='line' id='LC2112'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;autocmd BufNewFile,BufRead Templates  set filetype=template</div><div class='line' id='LC2113'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;autocmd BufNewFile,BufRead *.template  set filetype=template</div><div class='line' id='LC2114'>&nbsp;&nbsp;endif &quot; has(&quot;autocmd&quot;)</div><div class='line' id='LC2115'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2116'>The assignment defines the heading for the template section in the taglist</div><div class='line' id='LC2117'>window.  The autocmds set the file type &#39;template&#39; for the main template file</div><div class='line' id='LC2118'>&#39;Templates&#39; and the includefiles &#39;*.template&#39; (if any).</div><div class='line' id='LC2119'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2120'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2121'>8.  FOLDING                                                 *csupport-folding*</div><div class='line' id='LC2122'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2123'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2124'>This plugin can be used together with folding.</div><div class='line' id='LC2125'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2126'>There are a few peculiarities when the cursor is on a closed fold before</div><div class='line' id='LC2127'>inserting a template:</div><div class='line' id='LC2128'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2129'>Normal mode</div><div class='line' id='LC2130'>-----------</div><div class='line' id='LC2131'>Inserting blocks of complete lines below and above a fold (e.g. frame</div><div class='line' id='LC2132'>comments) and inserting at the top of a buffer (e.g. file description) works</div><div class='line' id='LC2133'>as usual.</div><div class='line' id='LC2134'>Insertions which go to the end of a line (e.g. end-of-line comments) and</div><div class='line' id='LC2135'>insertions which go to the cursor position (e.g. &#39;sizeof()&#39;) will be suppressed</div><div class='line' id='LC2136'>and a warning will be shown.</div><div class='line' id='LC2137'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2138'>Visual mode</div><div class='line' id='LC2139'>-----------</div><div class='line' id='LC2140'>A range of lines containing closed folds can be surrounded by constructs which</div><div class='line' id='LC2141'>have a visual mode, e.g. a for-loop: </div><div class='line' id='LC2142'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2143'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for ( ; ; ) {</div><div class='line' id='LC2144'>&nbsp;&nbsp;+---  4 lines: {------------------------------------------------------------</div><div class='line' id='LC2145'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</div><div class='line' id='LC2146'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2147'>See |folding| for more information on folding.</div><div class='line' id='LC2148'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2149'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2150'>9.  Additional Mappings                                 *csupport-ad-mappings*</div><div class='line' id='LC2151'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2152'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2153'>There are a few additional filetype specific key mappings defined in</div><div class='line' id='LC2154'>&#39;~/.vim/ftplugin/c.vim&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC2155'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2156'>Complete a classical C comment: &#39;/*&#39; =&gt; &#39;/* | */&#39; (modes: i,v).</div><div class='line' id='LC2157'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2158'>Complete a classical C multi-line comment (mode: i): </div><div class='line' id='LC2159'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&#39;/*&lt;CR&gt;&#39; =&gt;  /*</div><div class='line' id='LC2160'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* |</div><div class='line' id='LC2161'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*/</div><div class='line' id='LC2162'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2163'>Open a block (modes: i,v):</div><div class='line' id='LC2164'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&#39;{&lt;CR&gt;&#39; =&gt;  {</div><div class='line' id='LC2165'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;|</div><div class='line' id='LC2166'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</div><div class='line' id='LC2167'>In visual mode the content of the new block will be indented.</div><div class='line' id='LC2168'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2169'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2170'>10.  WINDOWS PARTICULARITIES                                *csupport-windows*</div><div class='line' id='LC2171'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2172'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2173'>For a user installation the plugin should go into the directory structure below </div><div class='line' id='LC2174'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$HOME/vimfiles/</div><div class='line' id='LC2175'>for a system installation below</div><div class='line' id='LC2176'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$VIM/vimfiles/</div><div class='line' id='LC2177'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2178'>The values of the two variables can be found from inside Vim:</div><div class='line' id='LC2179'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:echo $VIM</div><div class='line' id='LC2180'>or</div><div class='line' id='LC2181'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:echo $HOME</div><div class='line' id='LC2182'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2183'>The configuration files for a user are</div><div class='line' id='LC2184'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2185'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$HOME/_vimrc   and  $HOME/_gvimrc</div><div class='line' id='LC2186'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2187'>for the system</div><div class='line' id='LC2188'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2189'>&nbsp;&nbsp;$VIM/_vimrc   and  $VIM/_gvimrc</div><div class='line' id='LC2190'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2191'>Compiler settings:</div><div class='line' id='LC2192'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2193'>It could be necessary to add further settings for your compiler.  To compile</div><div class='line' id='LC2194'>C++-programs using a Dev-C++ installation (http://www.bloodshed.net) the</div><div class='line' id='LC2195'>following item in $VIM/_vimrc is needed (depends on the Dev-C++ install</div><div class='line' id='LC2196'>directory):</div><div class='line' id='LC2197'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2198'>&nbsp;&nbsp;let g:C_CFlags  = &#39;-Wall -g -o0 -c -I c:\programs\dev-c++\include\g++&#39;</div><div class='line' id='LC2199'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2200'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2201'>11.  ADDITIONAL TIPS                                           *csupport-tips*</div><div class='line' id='LC2202'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2203'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2204'>(1) gVim. Toggle &#39;insert mode&#39; &lt;--&gt; &#39;normal mode&#39; with the right mouse button</div><div class='line' id='LC2205'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(see mapping in file costumization.gvimrc).</div><div class='line' id='LC2206'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2207'>(2) gVim. Use tear off menus.</div><div class='line' id='LC2208'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2209'>(3) Try &#39;Focus under mouse&#39; as window behavior (No mouse click when the mouse</div><div class='line' id='LC2210'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;pointer is back from the menu item).</div><div class='line' id='LC2211'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2212'>(4) Use Emulate3Buttons &quot;on&quot; (X11) even for a 3-button mouse. Pressing left</div><div class='line' id='LC2213'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;and right button at the same time without moving your fingers is faster</div><div class='line' id='LC2214'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;then moving a finger to the middle button (often a wheel).</div><div class='line' id='LC2215'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2216'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2217'>12.  TROUBLESHOOTING                                *csupport-troubleshooting*</div><div class='line' id='LC2218'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2219'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2220'>* I do not see any new main menu item.</div><div class='line' id='LC2221'>&nbsp;&nbsp;- Was the archive extracted into the right directory?</div><div class='line' id='LC2222'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2223'>* How can I see what was loaded?</div><div class='line' id='LC2224'>&nbsp;&nbsp;- Use &#39;:scriptnames&#39; from the Vim command line.</div><div class='line' id='LC2225'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2226'>* No main menu item.</div><div class='line' id='LC2227'>&nbsp;&nbsp;- Loading of plugin files must be enabled. If not use</div><div class='line' id='LC2228'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;:filetype plugin on</div><div class='line' id='LC2229'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This is the minimal content of the file &#39;$HOME/.vimrc&#39;. Create one if there</div><div class='line' id='LC2230'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;is none, or better use customization.vimrc.</div><div class='line' id='LC2231'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2232'>* Most key mappings do not work.</div><div class='line' id='LC2233'>&nbsp;&nbsp;- They are defined in a filetype plugin in &#39;$HOME/.vim/ftplugin/&#39;. Use</div><div class='line' id='LC2234'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#39;:filetype&#39; to check if filetype plugins are enabled. If not, add the line</div><div class='line' id='LC2235'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;filetype plugin on</div><div class='line' id='LC2236'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;to the file &#39;~/.vimrc&#39;.</div><div class='line' id='LC2237'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2238'>* Some hotkeys do not work.</div><div class='line' id='LC2239'>&nbsp;&nbsp;- The hotkeys might be in use by your graphical desktop environment.  Under</div><div class='line' id='LC2240'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;KDE Ctrl-F9 is the hotkey which let you switch to the 9. desktop.  The key</div><div class='line' id='LC2241'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;settings can usually be redefined.</div><div class='line' id='LC2242'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2243'>* Splint and/or CodeCheck menu item not visible.</div><div class='line' id='LC2244'>&nbsp;&nbsp;- The program is not installed or not found (path not set) or not executable.</div><div class='line' id='LC2245'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2246'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2247'>13.  RELEASE NOTES                                    *csupport-release-notes*</div><div class='line' id='LC2248'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2249'>See file c-support/doc/ChangeLog .</div><div class='line' id='LC2250'><br/></div><div class='line' id='LC2251'>==============================================================================</div><div class='line' id='LC2252'>vim:tw=78:noet:ts=2:ft=help:norl:</div></pre></div></td>
         </tr>
       </table>
  </div>
